    <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 1-31]</head>

                <div n="1" type="adhyāya">



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||1|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha khalu bhagavantam amaravaram ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam āśramasthaṃ kāśirājaṃ
                        divodāsaṃ dhanvantarim aupadhenava<pc> </pc>vaitaraṇaurabhra<pc
                            > </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc> </pc>-karavīrya<pc> </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc
                            > </pc>suśruta<pc> </pc>prabhṛtaya ūcuḥ ||3|| <note type="footnote">
                            karavīra</note>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagavan śārīramānasāgantuvyādhibhir vividhavedanābhighātopadrutān sanāthān
                        apy anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś ca mānavān abhisamīkṣya manasi naḥ
                        pīḍā bhavati </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.4b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopaśamārtham ātmanaś ca prāṇayātrārthaṃ prajāhitahetor
                        āyurvedaṃ śrotum icchāma ihopadiśyamānaṃ atrāyattam aihikam āmuṣmikaṃ ca
                        śreyaḥ tad bhagavantam upapannāḥ smaḥ śiṣyatveneti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tān uvāca bhagavān svāgataṃ vaḥ sarva evāmīmāṃsyā adhyāpyāś ca bhavanto
                        vatsāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iha khalv āyurvedaṃ nāmopāṅgam atharvavedasyānutpādyaiva prajāḥ
                        ślokaśatasahasram adhyāyasahasraṃ ca kṛtavān svayambhūḥ tato 'lpāyuṣṭvam
                        alpamedhastvaṃ cālokya narāṇāṃ bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā praṇītavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā śalyaṃ śālākyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā kaumārabhṛtyaṃ
                        agadatantraṃ rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāsya pratyaṅgalakṣaṇasamāsaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.1a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śalyaṃ nāma
                        vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃśulohaloṣṭāsthibālanakhapūyāsrāvaduṣṭavraṇāntargarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ
                        yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānavraṇaviniścayārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śālākyaṃ nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānāṃ
                        vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāyacikītsā nāma sarvāṅgasaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                        jvararaktapittaśoṣonmādāpasmārakuṣṭhamehātisārādīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūtavidyā nāma
                        devāsuragandharvayakṣarakṣaḥpitṛpiśācanāgagrahādyupasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                        śāntikarmabaloharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaumārabhṛtyaṃ nāma kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīradoṣasaṃśodhanārthaṃ
                        duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthānāṃ ca vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         agadatantraṃ nāma sarpakīṭalūtāmūśikādidaṣṭaviṣavyañjanārthaṃ
                        vividhaviṣasaṃyogopaśamanārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanatantraṃ nāma vayaḥsthāpanam āyurmedhābalakaraṃ
                        rogāpaharaṇasamarthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vājīkaraṇatantraṃ nāmālpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasām
                        āpyāyanaprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ praharṣajananārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evam ayam āyurvedo 'ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate atra kasmai kim ucyatām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ūcuḥ asmākaṃ sarveṣām eva śalyajñānaṃ mūlaṃ kṛtvopadiśatu bhagavān iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa uvācaivam astv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ūcur bhūyo 'pi bhagavantam asmākam ekamatīnāṃ matam abhisamīkṣya suśruto
                        bhagavantaṃ prakṣyati asmai copadiśyamānaṃ vayam apy upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa hovācaivam astv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.14-16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vatsa suśruta iha khalv āyurvedaprayojanaṃ vyādhyupasṛṣṭānāṃ
                        vyādhiparimokṣaḥ svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ ca || āyur asmin vidyate 'nena vā+āyur
                        vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || tasyāṅgavaram ādyaṃ pratyakṣāgamānumānopamānair
                        aviruddham ucyamānam upadharaya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17.adda">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.17.adda</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etad dhy aṅgaṃ prathamaṃ prāg abhighātavraṇasaṃrohāt yajñaśiraḥsandhānāc ca
                        | śrūyate hi yathā rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam iti </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.17b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato devā aśvināv abhigamyocuḥ bhagavantau naḥ śreṣṭhatamau yuvāṃ
                        bhaviṣyathaḥ bhavadbhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ sandhātavyam iti | tāv ūcatur evam
                        astv iti | atha tayor arthe devā indraṃ yajñabhagena prāsādayan | tābhyāṃ
                        yajñasya śiraḥ saṃhitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāsv api cāyurvedatantreṣv etad evādhikam abhimataṃ āmāśu kriyākaraṇād
                        yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ vṛttikaraṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmā provāca tataḥ prajāpatir adhijage tasmād aśvinau aśvibhyām indraḥ
                        indrād aḥaṃ mayā tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra | ahaṃ hi dhanvantarir ādidevo jarārujāmṛtyuharo 'marāṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śalyāṅgam aṅgair aparair upetaṃ prāpto 'smi gāṃ bhūya ihopadeṣṭum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         asmin śāstre pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa ity ucyate | tasmin kriyā
                        so 'dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāt lokasya dvaividhyāt loko hi dvividhaḥ sthāvaro
                        jaṅgamaś ca dvividhātmaka evāgneyaḥ saumyaś ca tadbhūyastvāt pañcātmako vā
                        tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ saṃsvedajarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasaṃjñaḥ tatra
                        puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ tasyopakaraṇam anyat tasmāt puruṣo 'dhiṣṭhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad duḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya ucyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         te caturvidhāḥ āgantavaḥ śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ svābhāvikāś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣām āgantavo 'bhighātanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śārīrās tv annapānamūlā vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mānasās tu
                        krodhaśokabhayaharṣaviṣāderṣyābhyasūyādainyamātsaryakāmalobhaprabhṛtaya
                        icchādveṣabhedair bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svābhāvikās tu kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprakṛtayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ete manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyak prayuktā nigrahahetavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāṇināṃ punar mūlam āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattaḥ rasāḥ
                        punar dravyāśrayāḥ dravyāṇi punar oṣadhayaḥ | tās tu dvividhāḥ sthāvarā
                        jaṅgamāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāsāṃ sthāvarāś caturvidhāḥ vanaspatayo vṛkṣā vīrudha oṣadhaya iti | tāsu
                        apuṣpāḥ phalavanto vanaspatayaḥ puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ pratānavatyaḥ
                        stambinyaś ca vīrudhaḥ phalapākaniṣṭhā oṣadhaya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jaṅgamāḥ khalv api caturvidhāḥ jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjāḥ | tatra
                        paśumanuṣyavyālādayo jarāyujāḥ khagasarpasarīsṛpaprabhṛtayo 'ṇḍajāḥ
                            kṛmi<pc> </pc>kīṭa<pc> </pc>pipīlikā<pc> </pc>prabhṛtayaḥ svedajāḥ
                        indragopamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtaya udbhijjāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sthāvarebhyas tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandaniryāsasvarasādayaḥ
                        prayojanavantaḥ jaṅgamebhyaś carmanakharomarudhirādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pārthivāḥ suvarṇarajatamaṇimuktāmanaḥśilāmṛtkapālādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kālakṛtāḥ
                        pravātanivātātapacchāyājyotsnātamaḥśītoṣṇavarṣāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanādayaḥ
                        saṃvatsaraviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ete svabhāvata eva doṣāṇāṃ sañcayaprakopapraśamapratīkārahetavaḥ
                        prayojanavantaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         śārīrāṇāṃ vikārāṇām eṣa vargaś caturvidhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakope praśame caiva hetur uktaś cikitsakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantavas tu ye rogās te dvidhā nipatanti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasy anye śarīre 'nye teṣāṃ tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrapatitānāṃ tu śārīravad upakramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mānasānāṃ tu śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evam etat puruṣo vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyā kāla iti catuṣṭayaṃ samāsena
                        vyākhyātam | tatra puruṣagrahaṇāt tatsaṃbhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir uktas
                        tadaṅgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca tvaṅmāṃsāsthisirāsnāyuprabhṛtayaḥ vyādhigrahaṇād
                        vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ sarva eva vyādhayo vyākhyātāḥ
                        oṣadhagrahaṇād dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ kriyāgrahaṇāc chedyādīni
                        snehādīni ca karmāṇi vyākhyātāni kālagrahaṇāt sarvakriyākālānām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         bījaṃ cikitsitasyaitat samāsena prakīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam asya vyākhyā bhaviṣyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tac ca saviṃśam adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu
                        sūtranidānaśārīracikitsitakalpeṣv arthavaśāt saṃvibhajya uttare tantre śeṣān
                        arthān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayambhuvā proktam idaṃ sanātanaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭhed dhi yaḥ kāśipatiprakāśitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa puṇyakarmā bhuvi pūjito nṛpair
                        <caesura/>
                         asukṣaye śakrasalokatāṃ vrajet || </l>




                    <p xml:id="SS.1.1">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vedotpattir nāma prathamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ|]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ śiṣyopanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānām anyatamam anvaya<pc
                            > </pc>vayaḥ<pc/>śīla<pc> </pc>śaurya<pc> </pc>śaucācāra<pc
                            > </pc>vinaya<pc> </pc>śakti<pc> </pc>bala<pc> </pc>medhā<pc
                            > </pc>dhṛti<pc> </pc>smṛti<pc> </pc>mati<pc> </pc>pratipattiyuktaṃ
                            tanu<pc> </pc>jihvauṣṭha<pc> </pc>dantāgram ṛjuvaktrākṣināsaṃ
                        prasannacittavākceṣṭaṃ kleśasahaṃ ca bhiṣak śiṣyam upanayet ato
                        viparītaguṇaṃ nopanayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upanayanīyaṃ tu brāhmaṇaṃ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
                        praśastāyāṃ diśi śucau same deśe caturhastaṃ caturasraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya
                        gomayena darbhaiḥ saṃstīrya puṣpair lājabhaktai ratnaiś ca devatāḥ pūjayitvā
                        viprān bhiṣajaś ca tatrollikhyābhyukṣya ca dakṣiṇato brahmāṇaṃ
                        sthāpayitvā'gnim upasamādhāya khadirapalāśadevadārubilvānāṃ samidbhiś
                        caturṇāṃ vā kṣīravṛkṣāṇāṃ (? nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthamadhūkānāṃ )
                        dadhimadhughṛtāktābhir dārvīhaumikena vidhinā sruveṇājyāhutīr juhuyāt
                        sapraṇavābhir mahāvyahṛtibhiḥ tataḥ pratidaivatamṛṣīṃś ca svāhākāraṃ kuryāt
                        śiṣyam api kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brāhmaṇas trayāṇāṃ varṇānām upanayanaṃ kartum arhati rājanyo dvayasya
                        vaiśyo vaiśyasyaiveti śūdram api kulaguṇasaṃpannaṃ mantravarjam anupanītam
                        adhyāpayed ity eke || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'gniṃ triḥ pariṇīyāgnisākṣikaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāt
                        kāmakrodhalobhamohamānāhaṇkārerṣyāpāruṣyapaiśunyānṛtālasyāyaśasyāni hitvā
                        nīcanakharomṇā śucinā kaṣāyavāsasā
                        satyavratabrahmacaryābhivādanatatpareṇāvaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ
                        madanumatasthānagamanaśayanāsanabhojanādhyayanapareṇa bhūtvā matpriyahiteṣu
                        vartitavyaṃ ato 'nyathā te vartamānasyādharmo bhavati aphalā ca vidyā na ca
                        prākāśyaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ahaṃ vā tvayi samyagvartamāne yady anyathādarśī syām enobhāg bhaveyam
                        aphalavidyaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvijagurudaridramitrapravrajitopanatasādhvanāthābhyupagatānāṃ
                        cātmabāndhavānām iva svabhaiṣajaiḥ pratikartavyam evaṃ sādhu bhavati
                        vyādhaśākunikapatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca na pratikartavyaṃ evaṃ vidyā prakāśate
                            mitra<pc> </pc>yaśo<pc> </pc>dharmārtha<pc> </pc>kāmāṃś ca prāpnoti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra | kṛṣṇe 'ṣṭamī tannidhane 'hanī dve
                        <caesura/>
                         śukle tathāpy evam ahar dvisandhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         akālavidyutstanayitnughoṣe
                        <caesura/>
                         svatantrarāṣṭrakṣitipavyathāsu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śmaśānayānādyatanāhaveṣu
                        <caesura/>
                         mahotsavautpātikadarśaneṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nādhyeyam anyeṣu ca yeṣu vaprā
                        <caesura/>
                         nādhīyate nāśucinā ca nityam || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS1.2.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śiṣyopanayanīyo nāma
                        dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                        sūtrasthānamadhyāyāḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat ṣoḍśa nidānāni daśa śārīrāṇi
                        catvāriṃśaccikitsitāni aṣṭau kalpāḥ taduttaraṃ ṣaṭsāṣṭiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.4">

                         bhūtavidyeti catvāri tantre tūttarasaṃjñite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.45">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vājīkaraṃ cakitsāsu rasāyanavidhis tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣatantraṃ punaḥ kalpāḥ śalyajñānaṃ samantataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.46">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ity aṣṭāṅgam idaṃ tantram ādidevaprakāśitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhinā'dhītya yuñjānā bhavanti prāṇadā bhuvi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.47">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etad dhy avaśyam adhyeyaṃ adhītya ca karmāpy avaśyam upāsitavyaṃ ubhayajño
                        hi bhiṣak rājārho bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.48">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.48</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tu kevalaśāstrajñaḥ karmasva pariniṣṭhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa muhyaty āturaṃ prāpya prāpya bhīrur ivāhavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.49">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tu karmasu niṣṇāto dhārṣṭyāc chāstrabahiṣkṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa satsu pūjāṃ nāpnoti vadhaṃ cārhati rājataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.50">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ubhāv etāv anipuṇāv asamarthau svakarmaṇi |
                        <caesura/>
                         ardhavedadharāv etāv ekapakṣāv iva dvijau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.51">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣadhyo 'mṛtakalpās tu śastrāśaniviṣopamāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanty ajñair upahṛtās tasmād etān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.52">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.52</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehādiṣv anabhijñā ye chedyādiṣu ca karmasu |
                        <caesura/>
                         te nihanti janaṃ lobhāt kuvaidyā nṛpadoṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.53">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tūbhayajño matimān sa samartho 'rthasādhane |
                        <caesura/>
                         āhave karma nirvoḍhuṃ dvicakraḥ syandano yathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.54">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha vatsa tad etad adhyeyaṃ tathā tathopadhāraya mayā procyamānaṃ atha
                        śucaye kṛtottarāsaṅgāyāvyākulayopasthitāyādhyayanakāle śiṣyāya yathāśakti
                        gurur upadiśet padaṃ pādaṃ ślokaṃ vā te ca padapādaślokābhūyaḥ
                        krameṇānusaṃdheyāḥ evam ekaikaśo ghaṭayed ātmanā cānupaṭhet adrutam
                        avilambitam aviśaṇkitam ananunāsikaṃ vyaktākṣram apīḍitavarṇam
                        akṣibhruvauṣṭhahastair anabhinītaṃ susaṃskṛtaṃ nātyuccair nātinīcaiś ca
                        svaraiḥ paṭhet | na cāntareṇa kaścid vrajet tayor adhīyānayoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.55">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         śucir guruparo dakṣas tandrānidrāvivarjitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭhann etena vidhinā śiṣyaḥ śāstrāntam āpnuyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.56">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.56</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vāksauṣṭhave 'rthavijñāne prāgalbhye karmanaipuṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadabhyāse ca siddhau ca yatetādhyayanāntagaḥ || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāhaṃ sūtrasthāne 'dhyayanasaṃpradānīyo nāma
                        tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="4" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ prabhāṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yāthovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhigatam apy adhyayanam aprabhāṣitam arthataḥ kharasya candanabhāra iva
                        kevalaṃ pariśramakaraṃ bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kharaś candanabhāravāhī bhārasya vettā na tu candanasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ hi śāstrāṇi baḥūny adhītya cārtheṣu mūḍhāḥ kharavad vahanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam
                        anuśrotavyaṃ ca kasmāt sūkṣmā hi
                        dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākadoṣadhātumalāśayamarmasirāsnāyusandhyasthigarbhasaṃbhavadravyasamūhavibhāgās
                        tathā pranaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇavraṇaviniścayabhagnavikalpāḥ sādhyayāpy
                        apratyākhyeyatā ca vikārāṇām evam ādayaś cānye sahasraśo viśeṣā ye
                        vicintyamānā vimalavipulabuddher api buddhim ākulīkuryuḥ kiṃ punar
                        alpabuddheḥ tasmād avaśyam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam anuśrotavyaṃ
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anyaśāstropapannānāṃ cārthānām ihopanītānām arthavaśāt teṣāṃ tad vidyebhya
                        eva vyākhyānam anuśrotavyaṃ kasmāt na hy ekasmin śāstre śakyaḥ
                        sarvaśāstrāṇām avarodhaḥ kartum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaṃ śāstram adhīyāno na vidyāc chāstraniścayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād bahuśrutaḥ śāstraṃ vijānīyāc cikitsakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śāstraṃ gurumukhodgīrṇam ādāyopāsya cāsakṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ karma kurute vaiyaḥ sa vaidyo 'nye tu taskarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aupadhenavam aurabhraṃ sauśrutaṃ pauṣkalāvatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣāṇāṃ śalyatantrāṇāṃ mūlāny etāni nirdiśet || </l>

                    <p ana="1.4.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne prabhāṣanīyo nāma
                        caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                         hemante śiśire caiva vasante cāpi mokṣayet |

                         tryahāddvyahāccharadgrīṣmavarṣāsv api ca buddhimān || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="6" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>śaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta ṛtucaryam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kālo hi nāma bhagavān svayambhur anādimadhyanidhano 'tra rasavyāpatsampattī
                        jīvitamaraṇe ca manuṣyāṇām āyatte | sa sūkṣmām api kalāṃ na līyata iti kālaḥ
                        saṃkalayati kālayati vā bhūtānīti kālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya saṃvatsarātmano bhagavān ādityo gativiśeṣeṇa
                        nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrtāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasaṃvatsarayugapravibhāgaṃ
                        karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra laghvakṣaroccāraṇamātro 'kṣinimeṣaḥ pañcadaśā'kṣinimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhā
                        triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā viṃśatikalo muhūrtaḥ kalādaśabhāgaś ca triṃśanmuhūrtam
                        ahorātraṃ pañcadaśāhorātrāṇi pakṣaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca tau
                        māsaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra māghādayo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvimāsikam ṛtuṃ kṛtva ṣaḍṛtavo
                        bhavanti te śiśiravasantagrīṣmavarṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣaṃ tapastapsyau
                        śiśiraḥ madhumādhavau vasantaḥ śuciśukrau grīṣmaḥ nabhonabhasyau varśāḥ
                        iṣorjau śarat sahaḥsahasyau hemanta iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ete śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇāś candrād ity ayoḥ kālavibhāgakaratvād ayane dve
                        bhavato dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca | tayor dakṣiṇaṃ varṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣu
                        bhagavān āpyāyate somaḥ amlalavaṇamadhurāś ca rasā balavanto bhavanti
                        uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam abhivardhate | uttaraṃ ca
                        śiśiravasantagrīṣmāḥ teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate 'rkaḥ tiktakaṣāyakaṭukāś ca rasā
                        balavanto bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam apahīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītāṃśuḥ kledayaty urvīṃ vivasvān śoṣayaty api |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāv ubhāv api saṃśritya vāyuḥ pālayati prajāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha khalv ayane dve yugapat saṃvatsaro bhavati te tu pañca yugam iti
                        saṃjñāṃ labhante sa eṣa nimeṣādir yugaparyantaḥ kālaś cakravat
                        parivartamānaḥ kālacakram ucyata ity eke || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iha tu varṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmaprāvṛṣaḥ ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti
                        doṣopacayaprakopopaśamanimittaṃ te tu bhādrapadādyena dvimāsikena vyākhyātāḥ
                        tad yathā bhādrapadāśvayujau varṣāḥ kārtikamārgaśīrṣau śarat pauṣamāghau
                        hemantaḥ phālgunacaitrau vasantaḥ vaiśākhajyeṣṭhau grīṣmaḥ āṣāḍhaśrāvaṇau
                        prāvṛḍ iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra varṣāsv oṣadhayas taruṇyo 'lpavīryā āpaś cāprasannāḥ kṣitimalaprāyāḥ
                        tā upayujyamānā nabhasi meghāvatate jalapraklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ
                        prāṇināṃ śīta<pc> </pc>vāta<pc> </pc>viṣṭambhitāgnīnāṃ vidahyante vidāhāt
                        pittasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ śaradi praviralameghe viyaty upaśuṣyati
                        paṅke 'rka<pc> </pc>kiraṇa<pc> </pc>pravilāyitaḥ paittikān vyādhīn janayati
                        | tā evauṣadhayaḥ kālapariṇāmāt pariṇatavīryā balavatyo hemante bhavanty
                        āpaś ca prasannāḥ snigdhā atyarthaṃ gurvyaś ca tā upayujyamānā
                        mandakiraṇatvād bhānoḥ satuṣārapa<pc> </pc>vanopa<pc
                            > </pc>stambhita<pc> </pc>dehānāṃ dehinām avidagdhāḥ snehāc chaityād
                        gauravād upalepāc ca śleṣmasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayo vasante
                            'rka<pc> </pc>raśmi<pc> </pc>pravilāyita īṣatstabdhadehānāṃ dehināṃ
                        ślaiṣmikān vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayo nidāghe niḥsārā rūkṣā atimātraṃ
                        laghvyo bhavanty āpaś ca tā upayujyamānāḥ sūryapratāpopaśoṣitadehānāṃ
                        dehināṃ raukṣyāl laghutvād vaiśadyāc ca vāyoḥ saṃcayam āpādayanti sa
                        saṃcayaḥ prāvṛṣi cātyarthaṃ jalopaklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ
                        śītavātavarṣerito vātikān vyādhīn janayati | evam eṣa doṣāṇāṃ
                        saṃcayaprakopahetur uktaḥ ||</l>

                        viṃśatirnāḍyaḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ śalākāḥ panñcaviṃśatirupayantrāṇi || </l>

                        ca kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.13">

                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīyantrāṇi apyanekaprakārāṇi anekaprayojanāni ekatomukhānyubhayatomukhāni
                        ca tāni srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ rogadarśanārthaṃ ācūṣaṇārthaṃ
                        kriyāsaukaryārthaṃ ceti tāni srotodvārapariṇāhāni yathāyogadīrghāṇi ca |
                        tatra
                        bhagandarārśovraṇabastyuttarabastimūtravṛddhidakodaradhūmaniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudayantrāṇy
                        alābūśṛṅgayantrāṇi coprariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śalākāyantrāṇy api nānāprakārāṇi nānāprayojanāni yathāyogapariṇāhadīrghāṇi
                        ca teṣāṃ gaṇḍūpadasarpaphaṇaśarapuṅkhabaḍiśamukhe dve dve
                        eṣaṇavyūhanacālanāharaṇārtham upadiśyete masūradalamātramukhe dve
                        kiṃcidānatāgre srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ ṣaṭ kārpāsakṛtoṣṇīṣāṇi
                        pramārjanakriyāsu trīṇi darvyākṛtīni khallamukhāni
                        kṣārauṣadhapraṇidhānārthaṃ trīṇyanyāni jāmbavavadanāni trīṇyaṅkuśavadanāni
                        ṣaḍevāgnikarmasvabhipretāni nāsārbudaharaṇārthamekaṃ kolāsthidalamātramukhaṃ
                        khallatīkṣṇoṣṭhaṃ añjanārthamekaṃ kalāyaparimaṇḍalamubhuyato mukulāgraṃ
                        mūtramārgaviśodhanārthamekaṃ mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgrapramāṇaparimaṇḍalam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upayantrāṇyapi-rajjuveṇikāpaṭṭacarmāntavalkalalatāvastrāṣṭhīlāśmamudgarapāṇipādatalāṅgulijihvādantanakhamukhabālāśvakaṭakaśākhāṣṭhīvanapravāhaṇaharṣāyaskāntamayāni
                        kṣārāgnibheṣajāni ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etāni dehe sarvasmin dehasyāvayave tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃdhau koṣṭhe dhamanyāṃ ca yathāyogaṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yantrakarmāṇi tu
                        nirghātanapūraṇabandhanavyūhanavartanacālanavivartanavivaraṇapīḍanamārgaviśodhanavikarṣaṇāharaṇāñchanonnamanavinamanabhañjanonmathanācūṣaṇaiṣaṇadāraṇarjūkaraṇaprakṣālanapradhamanapramārjanāni
                        caturviṃśatiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabuddhyā cāpi vibhajedyantrakarmāṇi buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         asaṃkhyeyavikalpatvāc chalyānām iti niścayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra atisthūlaṃ asāraṃ atidīrghaṃ atihrasvaṃ agrāhi viṣamagrāhi vakraṃ
                        śithilaṃ atyunnataṃ mṛdukīlaṃ mṛdumukhaṃ mṛdupāśam iti dvādaśa yantradoṣāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etair doṣair vinirmuktaṃ yantramaṣṭādaśāṅgulam |
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastaṃ bhiṣajā jñeyaṃ taddhi karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛśyaṃ siṃhamukhādyais tu gūḍhaṃ kaṅkamukhādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirharet tu śanaiḥ śalyaṃ śa(ā.śā)strayuktivyapekṣayā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ni(ā.vi)vartate sādhvavagāhate ca śalyaṃ nigṛhyoddharate ca yasmāt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yantreṣv ataḥ kaṅkamukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣv adhi(ā.vi)kāri caiva
                        || </l>
                    <l ana="SS.1.7.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yantravidhirnāma
                        saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="8" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ śastrāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṃśatiḥ śastrāṇi; tad yathā— maṇḍalāgrakarapatra<pc
                            > </pc>vṛddhipatra<pc> </pc>nakhaśastra<pc
                            > </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhāra<pc> </pc>sūcī<pc
                            > </pc>kuśapatrāṭīmukha<pc> </pc>śarārimukhāntarmukha<pc
                            > </pc>trikūrcaka<pc> </pc>kuṭhārikā<pc> </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc
                            > </pc>vetasapatraka<pc> </pc>baḍiśa<pc> </pc>dantaśaṅkveṣaṇya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra maṇḍalāgrakarapatre syātāṃ chedane lekhane ca, vṛddhipatra<pc
                            > </pc>nakhaśastra<pc> </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhārāṇi chedane
                        bhedane ca, sūcīkuśapatrāṭī(ṭā)mukhaśarārimukhāntarmukhatrikūrcakāni
                        visrāvaṇe, kuṭhārikā<pc> </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc> </pc>vetasapatrakāṇi vyadhane
                        sūcī ca, baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cāharaṇe, eṣaṇy eṣaṇe ānulomye ca sūcyaḥ
                        sīvane; ity aṣṭavidhe karmaṇy upayogaḥ śastrāṇāṃ vyākkhyātaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣām atha yathāyogaṃ grahaṇasamāsopāyaḥ karmasu vakṣyate— tatra
                        vṛddhipatraṃ vṛntaphalasādhāraṇe bhāge gṛhṇīyāt, bhedanāny evaṃ sarvāṇi,
                        vṛddhipatraṃ maṇḍalāgraṃ ca kiṃcid uttānena pāṇinā lekhane bahuśo 'vacāryaṃ,
                        vṛntāgre visrāvaṇāni, viśeṣeṇa tu bālavṛddhasukumārabhīrunārīṇāṃ rājñāṃ
                        rājamā(pu)trāṇāṃ ca trikūrcakena visrāvayet, talapracchādita<pc> </pc>vṛntam
                        aṅguṣṭhapradeśinībhyāṃ vrīhimukhaṃ, kuṭhārikāṃ vāmahastanyastām
                            itarahastamadhyamāṅgulyā'ṅguṣṭhaviṣṭabdhay<pc> </pc>'bhihanyāt,
                        ārākarapatraiṣaṇyo mūle, śeṣāṇi tu yathāyogaṃ gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.7-8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.7-8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra nakhaśastraiṣaṇyāv aṣṭāṅgule, sūcyo vakṣyante,
                        (pradeśinyagraparvapradeśapramāṇā mudrikā, daśāṅgulā śarārimukhī sā ca (yā
                        sā) kartarīti kathyate |), śeṣāṇi tu ṣaḍaṅgulāni || tāni sugrahāṇi sulohāni
                        sudhārāṇi surūpāṇi susamāhitamukhāgrāṇi akarālāni ceti śastrasaṃpat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vakraṃ, kuṇṭhaṃ, khaṇḍaṃ, kharadhāram, atisthūlam, atyalpam,
                        atidīrgham, atihrasvam, ity aṣṭau śastradoṣāḥ | ato viparītaguṇam ādadīta,
                        anyatra karapatrāt; tad dhi kharadhāram asthicchedanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra dhārā bhedanānāṃ māsūrī, lekhanānām ardhamāsūrī, vyadhanānāṃ
                        visrāvaṇānāṃ ca kaiśikī, chedanānām ardhakaiśikīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cānatāgre | tīkṣṇakaṇṭakaprathamayavapatramukhyeṣaṇī
                        (gaṇḍūpadākāramukhī ca) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ pāyanā trividhā kśārodakataileṣu | tatra kṣārapāyitaṃ
                        śaraśalyāsthicchedaneṣu udakapāyitaṃ māṃsacchedanabhedanapāṭaneṣu
                        tailapāyitaṃ sirāvyadhanasnāyucchedaneṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ niśānārthaṃ ślakṣṇaśilā māṣavarṇā dhārāsaṃsthāpanārthaṃ
                        śālmalīphalakam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra—
                        <caesura/>
                         yadā suniśitaṃ śastraṃ romacchedi susaṃsthitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sugṛhītaṃ pramāṇena tadā karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anuśastrāṇi tu tvaksāra<pc> </pc>sphaṭika<pc> </pc>kāca<pc
                            > </pc>kuruvinda<pc> </pc>jalaukogni<pc
                        > </pc>kṣāranakhagojīśephālikāśākapatrakarīrabālāṅgulaya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śiśūnāṃ śastrabhīrūṇāṃ śastrābhāve ca yojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvaksārādicaturvargaṃ chedye ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āhārya<pc> </pc>cchedya<pc> </pc>bhedyeṣu nakhaṃ śakyeṣu yojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhiḥ pravakṣyate paścāt kṣāravahnijalaukasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye syur mukhagatā rogā netravartmagatāś ca ye |
                        <caesura/>
                         gojī<pc> </pc>śephālikā<pc> </pc>śākapatrair visrāvayet tu tān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣyeṣv eṣaṇyalābhe tu bālāṅgulyaṅkurā hitāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śastrāṇy etāni matimān śuddhaśaikyāyasāni tu ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kārayet karaṇaprāptaṃ karmāraṃ karmakovidam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prayogajñasya vaidyasya siddhir bhavati nity aśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt paricayaṃ kuryāc chastrāṇāṃ grahaṇe sadā || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śastrāvacāraṇīyo nāmāṣṭamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                <div n="9" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>navamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto yogyāsūtrīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhigatasarvaśāstrārtham api śiṣyaṃ yogyāṃ kārayet | snehādiṣu chedyādīṣu
                        ca karmapatham upadiśet | subahuśruto 'pyakṛtayogyaḥ karmasvayogyo bhavati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra puṣpaphalālābūkālindakatrapusai(ā.so)rvārukarkārukaprabhṛtiṣu
                        chedyaviśeṣān darśayet utkartanaparikartanāni copadiśet
                        dṛtibastiprasevakaprabhṛtiṣūdakapaṅkapūrṇeṣu bhedyayogyāṃ saromṇi
                        carmaṇyātate lekhyasya mṛtapaśusirāsūtpalanāleṣu ca vedhyasya
                        ghuṇopahatakāṣṭhaveṇunalanālīśuṣkālābūmukheṣveṣyasya
                        panasabimbībilvaphalamajjamṛtapaśudanteṣvāhāryasya madhūcchiṣṭopalipte
                        śālmalīphalake visrāvyasya sūkṣmaghanavastrāntayor mṛducarmāntayoś ca
                        sīvyasya pustamayapuruśāṅgapratyaṅgaviśeṣeṣu bandhanayogyāṃ
                        mṛducarmamāṃsapeśīṣūtpalanāleṣu ca karṇasandhibandhayogyāṃ mṛduṣu
                        māṃsakhaṇḍeṣv agnikṣārayogyāṃ udakapūṇaghaṭapārśvasrotasyalābūmukhādiṣu ca
                        netrapraṇidhānabastivraṇabastipīḍanayogyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.5ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         evam ādiṣu medhāvī yogyārheṣu yathāvidhi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.5cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyeṣu yogyāṃ kurvāṇo na pramuhyati karmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.6ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt kauśalam anvicchan śastrakṣārāgnikarmasu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.6cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya yatreha sādharmyaṃ tatra yogyāṃ samācaret || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yogyāsūtrīyo nāma navamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>



                <div n="10" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto viśikhānupraveśanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhigatatantreṇopāsitatantrārthena dṛṣṭakarmaṇā kṛtayogyena śāstraṃ
                        nigadatā rājānujñātena nīcanakharomṇā ṣucinā śuklavastraparihitena
                        chatravatā daṇḍahastena sopānatkenānuddhataveśena sumanasā
                        kalyāṇābhivyāhāreṇākuhakena bandhubhūtena bhūtānāṃ susahāyavatā vaidyena
                        niśikhā'nupraveṣṭavyā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato dūtanimittaśakunamaṅgalānulomyenātura<pc> </pc>gṛham abhigamya,
                        upaviśya, āturam abhipaśyet spṛśet pṛcchec ca; tribhir etair vijñānopāyai
                        rogāḥ prāyaśo veditavyā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ity eke tat tu na samyak ṣaḍvidho hi rogāṇāṃ vijñānopāyaḥ; tad yathā ---
                        pañcabhiḥ śrotrādibhiḥ praśnena ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śrotrendriyavijñeyā viśeṣā rogeṣu vraṇāsrāvanijñānīyādiṣu vakṣyante
                        tatra saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchati ity evam ādayaḥ
                        sparśanendriyavijñeyāḥ śītoṣṇaślakṣṇakarkaśamṛdukaṭhinatvād ayaḥ
                        sparśaviśeṣā jvaraśophādeṣu cakṣurindriyavijñeyāḥ
                        śarīropacayāpacayāyurlakṣaṇabalavarṇavikārādayaḥ rasanendriyavijñeyāḥ
                        pramehādiṣu rasaviśeṣāḥ ghrāṇendriyavijñeyā ariṣṭaliṅgādiṣu vraṇānām
                        avraṇānāṃ ca gandhaviśeṣāḥ praśnena ca vijānīyād deśaṃ kālaṃ jātiṃ sātmyam
                        ātaṅkasamutpattiṃ vedanāsamucchrāyaṃ balam antaragniṃ vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ
                        pravṛttyapravṛttī kālaprakarṣādīṃś ca viśeṣān | ātmasadṛśeṣu
                        vijñānābhyupāyeṣu tatsthānīyair jānīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyādṛṣṭā vikārā hi durākhyātās tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā duṣparimṛṣṭāś ca mohayeyuś cikitsakam || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.6ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yāpayet asādhyān nopakramet parisaṃvatsarotthitāṃś ca vikārān prāyaśo
                        varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sādhyā api vyādhayaḥ prāyeṇaiṣāṃ duścikitsyatamā bhavanti | tad yathā
                            śrotriyanṛpatistrībālavṛddhabhīru<pc> </pc>rājasevaka<pc
                            > </pc>kitavadrubala<pc> </pc>vaidyavidagdha<pc
                            > </pc>vyādhigopaka<pc> </pc>daridra<pc> </pc>kṛpaṇa<pc
                        > </pc>krodhanānām anātmavatām anāthānāṃ ca evaṃ nirūpya cikitsāṃ kurvan
                        dharmārthakāmayaśāṃsi prāpnoti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         strībhiḥ sahāsyāṃ saṃvāsaṃ parihāsaṃ ca varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattaṃ ca tābhyo nādeyam annād anyad bhiṣagvaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.trailer">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne viśikhānupraveśanīyo nāma daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        || </l>

                <div n="11" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ kṣārapākavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śastrānuśastrebhyaḥ kṣāraḥ pradhānatamaḥ chedyabhedyalekhyakaraṇāt
                        tridoṣaghnatvād viśeṣakriyāvacāraṇāc ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kṣaraṇāt kṣaṇanād vā kṣāraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nānauṣadhisamavāyāt tridoṣaghnaḥ śuklatvāt saumyaḥ tasya saumyasyāpi sato
                        dahanapacanadāraṇādiśaktiraviruddhā sa khalv āgneyauṣadhiguṇabhūyiṣṭhatvāt
                        kaṭuka uṣṇastīkṣṇaḥ pa(ā.pā)cano vilayanaḥ śodhano ropaṇaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ stambhano
                        lekhanaḥ kṛmyāmakaphakuṣṭhaviṣamedasām upahantā puṃstvasya cātisevitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa dvividhaḥ pratisāraṇīyaḥ pānīyaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pratisāraṇīyaḥ kuṣṭha<pc> </pc>kiṭibha<pc> </pc>dadru<pc
                            > </pc>maṇḍala<pc> </pc>kilāsa<pc> </pc>bhagandarārbudārśo<pc
                            > </pc>duṣṭa<pc> </pc>vraṇa<pc> </pc>nāḍī<pc> </pc>carma<pc
                            > </pc>kīla<pc> </pc>tilakālakanyaccha<pc> </pc>vyaṅga<pc
                            > </pc>maśaka<pc> </pc>bāhya<pc> </pc>vidradhi<pc> </pc>kṛmi<pc
                        > </pc>viṣādiṣūpadiśyate saptasu ca
                        mukharogeṣūpajihvādhijihvopakuśadantavaidarbheṣu tisṛṣu ca rohiṇīṣu eteṣv
                            evānuśastra<pc> </pc>praṇidhānam uktam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pānīyas tu
                        garagulmodarāgnisaṅgājīrṇārocakānāhaśarkarāśmaryābhyantaravidradhikṛmiviṣārśaḥsūpayujyate
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ahitas tu
                        raktapitta(ā.tti)jvaritapittaprakṛtibālavṛddhadurbalabhramamadamūrcchātimiraparītebhyo
                        'nyebhyaś caivaṃvidhebhyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ cetarakṣāravad dagdhvā parisrāvayet tasya vistaro 'nyatra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athetaras trividho mṛdurmadhyastīkṣṇaś ca | taṃ cikīrṣuḥ śaradi girisānujaṃ
                        śucir upoṣya praśaste 'hani praśastadeśajātam anupahataṃ madhyamavayasaṃ
                        mahāntamasitamuṣkakamadhivāsyāparedyuḥ pāṭayitvā svaṇḍaśaḥ prakalpyāvapāṭya
                        nirvāte deśe nicitiṃ kṛtvā sudhāśarkarāś ca prakṣipya nilanālair ādīpayet |
                        athopaśānte 'gnau tadbhasma pṛthaggṛhṇīyādbhasmaśarkarāś ca | athānenaiva
                        vidhānena
                        kuṭajapalāśāśvakarṇapāribhadrakabibhītakāragvadhatilvakārkasnuhyapāmārgapāṭalānaktamālavṛṣakadalīcitrakapūtīkendravṛkṣāsphotāśvamārakasaptacchadāgnimanthaguñjāś
                        catasraś ca kośātakīḥ samūlaphalapatraśākhā dahet | tataḥ kṣāradroṇam
                        udakadroṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir āloḍya mūtrair vā yathoktair ekaviṃśatikṛtvaḥ
                        parisrāvya mahati kaṭāhe śanair darvyāvaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yadā bhavaty
                        accho raktas tīkṣṇaḥ picchilaś ca tamādāya mahati vastre parisrāvyetaraṃ
                        vibhajya punar agnāv adhiśrayet | tata eva cakṣārodakāt kuḍavamadhyardhaṃ
                        vā'panayet | tataḥ kaṭaśarkarābhasmaśarkarākṣīrapākaśaṅkhanābhīragnivarṇāḥ
                        kṛtvā+āyase pātre tasminn eva kṣārodake niṣicya piṣṭvā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.11b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tenaiva dvidroṇe 'ṣṭapalasaṃmitaṃ śaṅkhānābhyādīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ prativāpya
                        satatam aprmattaś cainam avaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yathā nātisāndro
                        nātidravaś ca bhavati tathā prayateta | athainam āgatapākam avatāryānuguptam
                        āyase kumbhe saṃvṛtamukhe nidadhyād eṣa madhyamaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.12">

                        samāḥ ślakṣṇacūrṇāḥ śuktipramāṇāḥ pratīvāpaḥ | sa eva sapratīvāpaḥ pakvaḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.16">

                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.17">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.18">

                        nirīkṣyāvaghṛṣyāvalikhya pracchayitvā śalākayā kṣāraṃ pratisārayet dattvā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto 'gnikarmavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taddagdhānāṃ rogāṇām apunarbhāvād bheṣaja<pc> </pc>śastrakṣārair asādhyānāṃ
                        sat sādhyatvāc ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athemāni dahanopakaraṇāni tad yathā
                            pippalyajāśakṛdgodantaśaraśalākā<pc> </pc>jāmbavauṣṭhetaralauhāḥ
                        kṣaudraguḍasnehāś ca | tatra pippalyajāśakṛdgodantaśaraśalākās tvaggatānāṃ
                        jāmbavauṣṭhetaralauhā māṃsagatānāṃ kṣaudraguḍasnehāḥ
                        sirāsnāyusandhyasthigatānām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāgnikarma sarvartuṣu kuryād anyatra śaradgrīṣmābhyāṃ tatrāpyātyayike
                        'gnikarmasādhye vyādhau tat pratyanīkaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.6a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvavyādhiṣv ṛtuṣu ca picchilam annaṃ bhuktavataḥ (? karma kurvīta)
                        aśmarībhagandarārśomukharogeṣv abhuktavataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra dvividhamagnikarmāhureke tvagdagdhaṃ māṃsadagdhaṃ ca iha tu
                            sirāsnāyu<pc> </pc>sandhyasthiṣv api va pratiṣiddho 'gniḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śabdaprādurbhāvo durgandhatā tvaksaṃkocaś ca tvagdagdhe
                        kapotavarṇatā'lpaśvayathuvedanā śuṣkasaṃkucitavraṇatā ca māṃsadagdhe
                        kṛṣṇonnatavraṇatā srāvasannirodhaś ca sirāsnāyudagdhe rūkṣāruṇatā
                        karkaśasthiravraṇatā ca sandhyasthidagdhe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śirorogādhimanthayor bhrūlalāṭaśaṅkhapradeśeṣu dahet vartmarogeṣv
                        ārdrālaktakapraticchannāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ kṛvā vartmaromakūpān (? dahet ) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tvaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyusandhyasthisthite 'tyugraruji vāyāv
                        ucchritakaṭhinasupramāṃse vraṇe granthyarśo
                        'rbudabhagandarāpacīślīpadacarmakīlatilakālakāntravṛddhisandhisirācchedanādiṣu
                        nāḍīśoṇitātipravṛttiṣu cāgnikarma kuryāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra valaya-bindu-vilekhā-pratisāraṇānīti dahanaviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogasya saṃsthānamavekṣya samyaṅgarasya marmāṇi balābalaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhiṃ tathartuṃ ca samīkṣya samyak tato vyavasyed bhiṣagagnikarma || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra samyagdagdhe madhusarpirbhyām abhyaṅgaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athemānagninā pariharet pittaprakṛtim antaḥśoṇitaṃ
                        bhinnakoṣṭhamanuddhṛtaśalyaṃ durbalaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ bhīrumaneka<pc
                            > </pc>vraṇa<pc> </pc>pīḍitamasvedyāṃś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvamitarathādagdhalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ
                        va+āśritya dravyam agnir dahati agnisaṃtapto hi snehaḥ sūkṣmasirānusāritvāt
                        tvagādīn anupraviśyāśu dahati tasmāt snehadagdhe 'dhikā rujo bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.16a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pluṣṭaṃ durdagdhaṃ samyagdagdham atidagdhaṃ ceti caturvidham
                        agnidagdham | tatra yad vivarṇaṃ pluṣyate 'timātraṃ tat pluṣṭaṃ
                        yatrottiṣṭhanti sphoṭās tīvrāś coṣadāharāgapākavedanāś cirāc copaśāmyanti
                        tad drudagdhaṃ samyagdgdham anavagāḍhaṃ tālaphalavarṇaṃ susaṃsthitaṃ
                        pūrvalakṣaṇayuktaṃ ca atidagdhe māṃsāvalambanaṃ gātraviśleṣaḥ
                        sirāsnāyusandhyasthivyāpādanamatimātraṃ jvaradāhapipāsāmūrcchāś copadravā
                        bhavanti vraṇaś cāsya cireṇa rohati rūḍhaś ca vivarṇo bhavati | tad etac
                        caturvidham agnidagdhalakṣaṇam ātmakarma<pc> </pc>prasādhakaṃ(ā.naṃ) bhavati
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         agninā kopitaṃ raktaṃ bhṛśaṃ jantoḥ prakupyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatas tenaiva vegena pittam asyābhyudīryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tulyavīrye ubhe hyete rasato dravyatas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tenāsya vedanāstīvrāḥ prakṛtyā ca vidahyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.19ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sphoṭāḥ śīghraṃ prajāyante jvarastṛṣṇā ca vardhate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dagdhasyopaśamārthāya cikitsā saṃpravakṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pluṣṭasyāgnipratapanaṃ kāryamuṣṇaṃ tathauṣadham |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīre svinnabhūyiṣṭhe svinnaṃ bhavati śoṇitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṛtyā hyudakaṃ śītaṃ skandayatyatiśoṇitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt sukhayati hyuṣṇaṃ natu śītaṃ kathaṃcana || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītāmuṣṇāṃ ca durdagdhe kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtālepanasekāṃs tu śītānevāsya kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyagdagdhe tugākṣīrīplakṣacandanagairikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmṛtaiḥ sarpiṣā snigdhair ālepaṃ kārayed bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyānūpaudakaiś cainaṃ piṣṭair māṃsaiḥ pralepayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittavidradhivac cainaṃ santatoṣmāṇam ācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atidagdhe viśīrṇāni māṃsāny uddhṛtya śītalām |
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak paś cācchālitaṇḍulakaṇḍanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tindukītvakkapālair vā ghṛtamiśraiḥ pralepayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇaṃ guḍūcīpatrair vā chādayed athavaudakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāṃ ca nikhilāṃ kuryād bhiṣak pittavisarpavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhūcchiṣṭaṃ samadhukaṃ rodhraṃ sarjarasaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhāṃ cadanaṃ mūrvāṃ piṣṭvā sarpir vipācayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣāmagnidagdhānām etad ropaṇam uttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.29ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehadagdhe kriyāṃ rūkṣāṃ viśeṣeṇāvacārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.12.29cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dhūmopahatalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvasiti kṣauti cātyarthamatyādhamati kāsate |
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuṣoḥ paridāhaś ca rāgaś caivopajāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhūmakaṃ niśvasiti ghreyamanyanna vetti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathaiva ca rasān sarvān śrutiś cāsyopahanyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.32abc</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇādāhajvarayutaḥ sīdaty atha ca mūrcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmopahata ity evaṃ śṛṇu tasya cikitsitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirikṣurasaṃ drākṣāṃ payo vā śarkarāmbu vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurāmlau rasau vā'pi vamanāya pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vamataḥ koṣṭhaśuddhiḥ syāddhūmagandhaś ca naśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhinā'nena śāmyanti sadanakṣavathujvarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāha<pc> </pc>mūrcchā<pc> </pc>tṛḍādhmāna<pc> </pc>śvāsakāsāś ca dāruṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurair lavaṇāmlaiś ca kaṭukaiḥ kavalagrahaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.36ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag gṛhṇātīndriyārthān manaś cāsya prasīdati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.12.36cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai dadyād yogena śāstravit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭir viśudhyate cāsya śirogrīvaṃ ca dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avidāhi laghu snigdhamāhāraṃ cāsya kalpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇavātātapair dagdhe śītaḥ kāryo vidhiḥ sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītavarṣānilair dagdhe snigdhamuṣṇaṃ ca śasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā'titejasā dagdhe siddhir nāsti kathaṃcana |
                        <caesura/>
                         indravajrāgnidaghe 'pi jīvati pratikārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        'gnikarmavidhair nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
