                <div n="13" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <note xml:lang="en">The vulgate text here in adhyāya 13 is transcribed from the
                        1938 edition, not the 1931 edition.</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto jalaukāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.2">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.3">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛpāḍhya<pc> </pc>bāla<pc> </pc>sthavira<pc> </pc>bhīru<pc> </pc>durbala<pc> </pc>nārī<pc> </pc>sukumārāṇām
                        anugrahārthaṃ paramasukumāro 'yaṃ śoṇitāvasecanopāyo 'bhihito jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.4">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātapittakaphaduṣṭaśoṇitaṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir
                        avasecayet sarvāṇi sarvair vā (viśeṣas tu visrāvyaṃ śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir
                        gṛhṇīyāt) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.5">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaṃ samadhuraṃ snigdhaṃ gavāṃ śṛṅgaṃ prakīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād vātopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.6">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītādhivāsā madhurā jalaukā vārisaṃbhavā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt pittopasṛṣṭe tu hitā sā tv avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.7">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alābu kaṭukaṃ rūkṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca parikīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāc chleṣmopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pracchite tanu<pc> </pc>basti<pc> </pc>paṭalāvanaddhena śṛṅgeṇa
                        śoṇitam avasecayed ācūṣaṇāt sāntardīpayā 'lābvā | (jalāyukā vakṣyante) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jalam āsām āyur iti jalāyukāḥ jalam āsām oka iti jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tā dvādaśa tāsāṃ saviṣāḥ ṣaṭ tāvatya eva nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.11">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra saviṣāḥ kṛṣṇā karburā alagardā indrāyudhā sāmudrikā gocandanā ceti |
                        tāsu añjanacūrṇavarṇā pṛthuśirāḥ kṛṣṇā varmimatsyavad āyatā
                        chinnonnatakukṣiḥ karburā romaśā mahāpārśvā kṛṣṇamukhī alagardā
                        indrāyudhavad ūrdhvarājibhiś citritā indrāyudhā īṣadasitapītikā
                        vicitrapuṣpākṛticitrā sāmudrikāḥ govṛṣaṇavad adhobhāge dvidhābhūtākṛtir
                        aṇumukhī gocandaneti | tābhir daṣṭe puruṣe daṃśe śvayathur atimātraṃ
                        kaṇḍūrmūrcchā jvaro dāhaś chardir madaḥ sadanam iti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra
                        mahāgadaḥ pānālepananasya karmādiṣūpayojyaḥ | indrāyudhādaṣṭam asādhyam |
                        ity etāḥ saviṣāḥ sacikitsitā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.12">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha nirviṣāḥ kapilā piṅgalā śaṅkumukhī mūṣikā puṇḍarīkamukhī sāvarikā ceti
                        | tatra manaḥśilārañjitābhyām iva pārśvābhyāṃ pṛṣṭhe snigdhā mudgavarṇā
                        kapilā kiṃcidraktā vṛttakāyā piṅgalā ''śugā ca piṅgalā yakṛdvarṇā
                        śīghrapāyinī dīrghatīkṣṇamukhī śaṅkumukhīḥ mūṣikākṛtivarṇā 'niṣṭagandhā ca
                        mūṣikā mudgavarṇā puṇḍarīkatulyavaktrā puṇḍarīkamukhī snigdhā
                        padmapatravarṇā 'ṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇā sāvarikā sā ca paśvarthe ity etā aviṣā
                        vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.13">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāsāṃ yavanapāṇḍyasahya<pc> </pc>pautanādīni kṣetrāṇi teṣu mahāśarīrā
                        balavatyaḥ śīghrapāyinyo mahāśanā nirviṣāś ca viśeṣeṇa bhavanti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.14">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra saviṣa<pc> </pc>matsya<pc> </pc>kīṭa<pc> </pc>dardura<pc
                            > </pc>mūtra<pc> </pc>purīṣa<pc> </pc>kothajātāḥ kaluṣeṣv ambhaḥsu ca
                        saviṣāḥ padmotpala<pc> </pc>nalina<pc> </pc>kumuda<pc
                            > </pc>saugandhika<pc> </pc>kuvalaya<pc> </pc>puṇḍarīka<pc
                            > </pc>śaivala<pc> </pc>kotha<pc> </pc>jātā vimaleṣv ambhaḥsu ca
                        nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.15">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣetreṣu vicaranty etāḥ salilāḍhyasugandhiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca saṃkīrṇacāriṇyo na ca paṅkeśayāḥ sukhāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.16">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāsāṃ grahaṇam ārdracarmaṇā, anyair vā prayogair gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.17">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athaināṃ nave mahati ghaṭe sarastaḍāgodakapaṅkam āvāpya nidadhyāt
                        bhakṣyārthe cāsām upaharec chaivalaṃ vallūram audakāṃś ca kandāṃś cūrṇīkṛtya
                        śayyārthaṃ tṛṇam audakāni ca patrāṇi tryahāt tryahāc cābhyo 'nyaj jalaṃ
                        bhakṣyaṃ ca dadyāt saptarātrāt saptarātrāc ca ghaṭam anyaṃ saṃkrāmayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.18">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlamadhyāḥ parikliṣṭāḥ pṛthvyo mandaviceṣṭitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         agrāhiṇyo 'lpapāyinyaḥ saviṣāś ca na pūjitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.19">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha jalauko 'vasekasādhyavyādhitam upaveśya saṃveśya vā virūkṣya cāsya tam
                        avakāśaṃ mṛdgomayacūrṇair yady arujaḥ syāt | gṛhītāś ca tāḥ
                            sarṣaparajanī<pc> </pc>kalkodaka<pc> </pc>pradigdha<pc> </pc>gātrīḥ
                        salilasarakamadhye muhūrtasthitā vigataklamā jñātvā tābhī rogaṃ grāhayet |
                        ślakṣṇaśuklārdrapicuprotāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā mukham apāvṛṇuyāt agṛhṇantyai
                        kṣīrabinduṃ śoṇitabinduṃ vā dadyāt, śastrapadāni vā kurvīta yady evam api na
                        gṛhṇīyāt tadā'nyāṃ grāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.20">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yadā ca niviśate 'śvakhuravad ānanaṃ kṛtvonnamya ca skandhaṃ tadā jānīyād
                        gṛhṇātīti gṛhṇantīṃ cārdravastrāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.21">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daṃśe toda<pc> </pc>kaṇḍu<pc> </pc>prādur<pc> </pc>bhāvair jānīyāc chuddham
                        iyam ādatta iti śuddham ādadānām apanayet atha śoṇitagandhena na muñcen
                        mukham asyāḥ saindhavacūrṇenāvakiret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22a">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.22a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha patitāṃ taṇḍula<pc> </pc>kaṇḍana<pc> </pc>pradigdhagātrīṃ
                        tailalavaṇābhyaktamukhīṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṃ gṛhītapucchāṃ
                        dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ śanaiḥ śanair anulomam anumārjayed ā mukhāt
                        vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti | samyagvāntā
                            salilasarake<pc> </pc>nyastā bhoktukāmā satī caret | yā sīdatī na
                        ceṣṭate sā durvāntā tāṃ punaḥ samyag vāmayet | durvāntāyā vyādhir asādhya
                        indramado nāma bhavati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22b">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.22b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha suvāntāṃ pūrvavat sannidadhyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṇitasya yogāyogān avekṣya śatadhautaghṛtābhyaṅgas tat picudhāraṇaṃ vāi
                        jalaukovraṇān madhunā'vaghaṭṭayet śitābhir adbhiś pariṣecayed badhnīta vā
                        kaṣāyamadhurasnigdhaśītaiś ca pradehaiḥ pradihyād iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.24">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra | kṣetrāṇi grahaṇaṃ jātīḥ poṣaṇaṃ sāvacāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaukasāṃ ca yo vetti tat sādhyān sa jayed gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne jalaukāvacāraṇīyo
                        nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>

                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ śoṇitavarṇanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pāñcabhautikasya caturvidhasya ṣaḍrasasya
                        dvividhavīryasyāṣṭavidhāvīryasya vā'nekaguṇasyopayuktasyāhārasya
                        samyakpariṇatasya yas tejobhūtaḥ sāraḥ paramasūkṣmaḥ sa rasa ity ucyate
                        tasya ca hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ sa hṛdayāc caturviṃśati dhamanīr anupraviśyor
                        dhvagā daśa daśa cādhogāminyaś catasraś ca tiryaggāḥ kṛtsnaṃ śarīram
                        aharahas tarpayati vardhayati dhārayati yāpayati cādṛṣṭahetukena karmaṇā |
                        tasya śarīram anusarato 'numānād gatir upalakṣayitavyā kṣayavṛddhivaikṛtaiḥ
                        | tasmin sarvaśarīrāvayavadoṣadhātumalāśayānusāriṇi rase jijñāsā kim ayaṃ
                        saumyas taijasa iti | atrocyate sa khalu dravānusārī
                        snehanajīvanatarpaṇadhāraṇādibhir viśeṣaiḥ saumya ity avagamyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa khalv āpyo raso yakṛtplīhānau prāpya rāgam upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         rañjitās tejasā tv āpaḥ śarīrasthena dehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         avyāpannāḥ prasannena raktam ity abhidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasād eva striyā raktaṃ rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ pravartate | tad varṣād dvyādaśād
                        ūrdhvaṃ yāti pañcāśataḥ kṣayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ārtavaṃ śoṇitaṃ tv āgneyaṃ agnīṣomīyatvād garbhasya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāñcabhautikaṃ tv apare jīvaraktam āhur ācāryāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         visratā dravatā rāgaḥ spandanaṃ laghutā tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūmyādīnāṃ guṇā hyete dṛśyante cātra śoṇite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasād raktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medaḥ prajāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         medaso 'sthi tato majjā majjñaḥ śukraṃ tu jāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraiṣāṃ (? sarva ) dhātūnām annapānarasaḥ prīṇayitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasajaṃ puruṣaṃ vidyād rasaṃ rakṣet prayatnaḥ | annāt pānāc ca matimān

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.18">

                        naivā(ā.naiva cā)stīti athavā'(? ca)sti satāṃ bhāvānām abhivyaktir iti

                        kālāntareṇābhivyaktiṃ gacchati evaṃ bālānām api vayaḥpariṇāmāc

                        phanilamaruṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ parūṣaṃ tanu śīghragamaskandi ca vātena duṣṭaṃ nīlaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.36">

                        rodhramadhukapriyaṅgupattaṅgagairikasarjarasarasāñjanaśālmalīpuṣpaśaṅkhaśuktimāṣayavagodhūmacūrṇaiḥ
                        śanaiḥ śanair vraṇamukham avacūrṇyāṅgulyagreṇāvapīḍayet
                        sālasarjārjūnārimedameṣaśṛnṅgadhavadhanvantvagbhir vā cūrṇitābhiḥ kṣaumeṇa
                        vā dhmāpitena samudraphenalākṣācūrṇair vā yathoktair vraṇabandhanadravyair

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.1">

                        pravibhaktaḥ śarīraṃ dhārayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.2">

                        agnikarmaṇānugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.4.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhisaṃśleṣaṇasnehanaropaṇapūraṇabalasthairyakṛcchleṣmā pañcadhā
                        pravibhakta udakakarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasas tuṣṭiṃ prīṇanaṃ raktapuṣṭiṃ ca karoti raktaṃ varṇaprasādaṃ
                        māṃsapuṣṭiṃ jīvayati ca māṃsaṃ śarīrapuṣṭiṃ medasaś ca medaḥ snehasvedau
                        dṛḍhatvaṃ puṣṭim asthnāṃ ca asthīni dehadhāraṇaṃ majjñaḥ puṣṭiṃ ca majjā
                        prītiṃ snehaṃ balaṃ śukrapuṣṭiṃ pūraṇam asthnāṃ ca karoti śukraṃ dhairyaṃ
                        cyavanaṃ prītiṃ dehabalaṃ harṣaṃ bījārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         purīṣam upastambhaṃ vāyvagnidhāraṇaṃ ca bastipūraṇavikledakṛn mūtraṃ svedaḥ
                        kledatvaksaukumāryakṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         raktalakṣaṇam ārtavaṃ garbhakṛc ca garbho garbhalakṣaṇaṃ stanyaṃ stanayor
                        āpīnatvajananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vidhivat parirakṣaṇaṃ kurvīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvam eṣāṃ kṣīṇalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra vātakṣaye
                        mandaceṣṭatā'lpāvāktvam apraharṣo mūḍhasaṃjñatā ca pittakṣaye mandoṣmāgnitā
                        niṣprabhatvaṃ(ā.tā) ca śleṣmakṣaye rūkṣatā'ntardāha
                        āmāśayetaraśleṣmāśayaśūnyatā sandhiśaithilyaṃ tṛṣṇā daurbalyaṃ prajāgaraṇaṃ
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.10">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakṣaye hṛtpīḍā<pc> </pc>kampaśūnyātās tṛṣṇā ca śoṇitakṣaye tvakpāruṣyam
                        amlaśītaprārthanā sirāśaithilyaṃ ca māṃsakṣaye
                            sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthoruvakṣaḥ<pc> </pc>kakṣāpiṇḍikodaragrīvāśuṣkatā
                        raukṣyatodau gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ dhamanīśaithilyaṃ ca medaḥkṣaye
                        plīhābhivṛddhiḥ sandhiśūnyatā raukṣyaṃ meduramāṃsaprārthanā ca asthikṣaye
                        'sthiśūlaṃ dantanakhabhaṅgo raukṣyaṃ ca majjakṣaye 'lpaśukratā parvabhedo
                        'sthinistodo 'sthiśūnyatā ca śukrakṣaye meḍhravṛṣaṇavedanā'śaktirmaithune
                        cirād vā prasekaḥ praseke cālparaktaśukradarśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāpi svayonivardhanadravyopayogaḥ pratīkāraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         purīṣakṣaye hṛdayapārśvapīḍā saśabdasya ca vāyor ūrdhvagamanaṃ kukṣau
                        saṃcaraṇaṃ ca mūtrakṣaye bastitodo 'lpamūtratā ca atrāpi
                        svayonivardhanadravyāṇi pratīkāraḥ | svedakṣaye stabdharomakūpatā tvakśoṣaḥ
                        sparśavaiguṇyaṃ svedanāśaś ca tatrābhyaṅgaḥ svedopayogaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ārtavakṣaye yathocitakālādarśanamalpatā vā yonivedanā ca tatra
                        saṃśodhanamāgneyānāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ vidhivad upayogaḥ | stanyakṣaye stnayor
                        mlānatā stanyāsaṃbhavo 'lpatā vā tatra śleṣmavardhanadravyopayogaḥ |
                        garbhakṣaye garbhāspandanamanunnatakukṣitā ca tatra prāptabastikālāyāḥ
                        kṣīrabastiprayogo medhyānnopayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvam ativṛddhānāṃ doṣadhātumalānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | vṛddhiḥ
                        punar eṣāṃ svayonivardhanāty upasevanād bhavati | tatra vātavṛddhau
                        vākpāruṣyaṃ kārśyaṃ kārṣṇyaṃ gātrasphuraṇam uṣṇakāmitā nidrānāśo
                        'lpabalatvaṃ gāḍhavarcastvaṃ ca pittavṛddhau pītāvabhāsatā saṃtāpaḥ
                        śītakāmitvam alpanidratā mūrcchā balahānir indriyadaurbalyaṃ
                        pītaviṇmūtranetratvaṃ ca śleṣmavṛddhau śauklyaṃ śaityaṃ sthairyaṃ gauravam
                        avasādas tandrā nidrā sandhyasthiviśleṣaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         raso 'tivṛddho hṛdayotkledaṃ prasekaṃ cāpādayati raktaṃ raktāṅgākṣitāṃ
                        sirāpūrṇatvaṃ ca māṃsaṃ sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthorubāhujaṅghāsu vṛddhiṃ
                        gurugātratāṃ ca medaḥ snigdhāṅgatāmudarapārśvavṛddhiṃ kāsaśvāsādīn
                        daurgandhyaṃ ca asthyadhyasthīnyadhidantāṃś ca majjā sarvāṅganetragauravaṃ
                        ca śukraṃ śukrāśmarīmatiprādurbhāvaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         purīṣamāṭopaṃ kukṣau śūlaṃ ca mūtraṃ mūtravṛddhiṃ muhurmuhuḥ pravṛttiṃ
                        bastitodamādhmānaṃ ca svedastvaco daugandhyaṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ārtavam aṅgamardam atipravṛttiṃ daurgandhyaṃ ca stanyaṃ stanayor āpīnatvaṃ
                        muhur muhuḥ pravṛttiṃ todaṃ ca garbho jaṭharābhivṛddhiṃ svedaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ yathāsvaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ kṣapaṇaṃ ca kṣayād aviruddhaiḥ kriyāviśeṣaiḥ
                        prakurvīt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvaḥ pūrvo 'tivṛddhatvād vardhayed dhi paraṃ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasam ātipravṛddhānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hrāsanaṃ hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balalakṣaṇaṃ balakṣayalakṣaṇaṃ cāta ūrdhvam upadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra rasādīnāṃ
                        śukrāntānāṃ dhātūnāṃ yat paraṃ tejas tat khalv ojas tad eva balam ity ucyate
                        svaśāstrasiddhāntāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra balena sthiropacitamāṃsatā sarvaceṣṭāsvapratighātaḥ svaravarṇaprasādo
                        bāhyānām ābhyantarāṇāṃ ca karaṇānām ātmakāryapratipattir bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         ojaḥ somātmakaṃ snigdhaṃ śuklaṃ śītaṃ sthiraṃ saram |
                        <caesura/>
                         viviktaṃ mṛdu mṛtsnaṃ ca prāṇāyatanam utttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.24ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dehaḥ sāvayavas tena vyāpto bhavati dehinām |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.24cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tadabhāvāc ca śīryante śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25abcd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.25abcd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhighātāt kṣayāt kopāc chokād dhyānāc chramāt kṣudhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ojaḥ saṃkṣīyate hy ebhyo dhātugrahaṇaniḥsṛtam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.25ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tejaḥ samīritaṃ tasmād visraṃsayate dehinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.26-27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.26-27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya visraṃso vyāpat kṣaya iti liṅgāni vyāpannasya bhavanti sandhiviśleṣo
                        gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ doṣacyavanaṃ kriyā'(O.kriyā)sannirodhaś ca visraṃse
                        stabdhagurugātratā vātaśopho varṇabhedo glānis tandrā nidrā ca vyāpanne
                        mūrcchā māṃsakṣayo mohaḥ pralāpo maraṇam iti ca kṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayo doṣā balasyoktā vyāpadvisraṃsanakṣayāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśleṣasādau gātrāṇāṃ doṣavisraṃsanaṃ śramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aprācuryaṃ kriyānāṃ ca balavisraṃsalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gurutvaṃ stabdhatā'ṇgeṣu glānirvarṇasya bhedanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tandrā nidrā vātaśopho balavyāpadi lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchā māṃsakṣāyo mohaḥ pralāpo 'jñānam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvoktāni ca liṅgāni maraṇaṃ ca balakṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra visraṃse vyāpanne ca kriyāviśeṣair aviruddhair balamāpyāyayet itaraṃ
                        tu mūḍhasaṃjñaṃ varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣadhātumalakṣīṇo balakṣīṇi'pi vā naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayonivardhanaṃ yattadannapānaṃ prakāṅkṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yadyadāhārajātaṃ tu kṣīṇaḥ prārthayate naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tasya sa lābhe tu taṃ taṃ kṣayamapohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya dhātukṣayād vāyuḥ saṃjñāṃ karma ca nāśayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣiṇaṃ ca balaṃ yasya nāsu śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasanimittam eva sthaulyaṃ kārśyaṃ ca | tatra śleṣmalāhārasevino
                        'dhyaśanaśīlasyāvyāyāmino divāsvapnaratasya cāma evānnaraso madhurataraś ca
                        śarīram anukrāmann atisnehān medo janayati tad atisthaulyam āpādayati tam
                        atisthūlaṃ
                        kṣudraśvāsapipāsākṣutsvapnasvedagātradaurgandhyakrathanagātrasādagadgadatvāni
                        kṣipram evāviśanti saukumāryān medasaḥ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaḥ kaphamedo
                        niruddhamārgartvāc cālpavyavāyo bhavati āvṛtamārgatvād eva śeṣā dhātavo
                        nāpyāyante 'tyarthamato 'lpaprāṇo bhavati
                        pramehapīḍakājvarabhagandaravidradhivātavikārāṇāmanyataṃ prāpya pañcatvam
                        upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty āvṛtamārgatvāt srotasāṃ atas
                        tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                        śilājatuguggulugomūtratriphalāloharajorasāñjanamadhuyavamudgakoradūṣakaśyāmākoddālakādīnāṃ
                        virūkṣaṇacchedanīyānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ vidhivad upayogo vyāyāmo
                        lekhanabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra punar vātalāhārasevino
                        'tivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanabhayaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇapipāsākṣutkaṣāyālpāśanaprabhṛtibhir
                        upaśoṣito rasadhātuḥ śarīram ananukrāman nalpatvān na prīṇāti tasmād
                        atikārśyaṃ bhavati so 'tikṛśaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavātavarṣabhārādāneṣv
                        asahiṣṇur vātarogaprāyo 'lpaprāṇaś ca kriyāsu bhavati
                        śvāsakāsaśoṣaplīhodarāgnisādagulmaraktapittānām anyatamam āsādya maraṇam
                        upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty alpaprāṇatvāt atas
                        tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                        payasyāśvagandhāvidārigandhāśatāvarībalātibalānāgabalānāṃ madhurāṇām anyāsaṃ
                        cauṣadhīnām upayogaḥ kṣīradadhighṛtamāṃsaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānāṃ ca
                        divāsvapnabrahmacaryāvyāyāmabṛhaṇabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ punar ubhayasādhāraṇāny āseveta tasyān narasaḥ śarīram anukrāman samān
                        dhātūn upacinoti samadhātutvān madhyaśarīro bhavati sarvakriyāsu samarthaḥ
                        kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavarṣātapasaho balavāṃś ca sa satatam anupālayitavya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyantagarhitāv etau sadā sthūlakṛśau narau |
                        <caesura/>
                         śreṣṭho madhyaśarīras tu kṛśaḥ sthūlāt tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaḥ prakupito dhātūn kṣapayaty ātmatejasā |
                        <caesura/>
                         iddhaḥ svatejasā vahnir ukhāgatam ivodakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vailakṣaṇyāc charīrāṇām asthāyitvāt tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣadhātumalānāṃ tu parimāṇaṃ na vidyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣāṃ samatvaṃ yac cāpi bhiṣagbhir avadhāryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         na tat svāsthyādṛte śakyaṃ vaktum anyena hetunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣādīnāṃ tv asamatām anumānena lakṣayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         aprasannendriyaṃ vīkṣya puruṣaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ kuryād asvasthasya tu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣapayed bṛṃhayec cāpi doṣadhātumalān bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāvad yāvad arogaḥ syād etat sāmyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samadoṣaḥ samāgniś ca samadhātumalakriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasannātmendriyamanāḥ svasthā ity abhidhīyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣābhūṣaṇanimittaṃ bālasya karṇau vidhyete | tau ṣaṣṭhe māsi saptame vā
                        śuklapakṣe praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaṃ
                        dhātryaṅke kumāradharāṅke vā kumāram upaveśya bālakrīḍanakaiḥ
                        pralobhyābhisāntvayan bhiṣag vāmahastenākṛṣya karṇaṃ daivakṛte chidra
                        ādityakarāvabhāsite śanaiḥ śanair dakṣiṇahastena rju vidhyet pratanukaṃ
                        sūcyā bahalam ārayā pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kumārasya vāmaṃ kumāryāḥ tataḥ
                        picuvartiṃ praveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.4</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        nirupadravatayā taddeśaviddham iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrājñena yadṛcchayā viddhāsu sirāsu kālikāmarmarikālohitikāsūpadravā
                        bhavanti | tatra kālikāyāṃ jvaro dāhaḥ śvayathur vedanā ca bhavati
                        marmarikāyāṃ vedanā jvaro granthayaś ca lohitikāyāṃ
                        manyāstambhāpatānakaśirograhakarṇaśūlāni bhavanti | teṣu yathāsvaṃ
                        pratikurvīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kliṣṭajihmāpraśastasūcīvyadhād gāḍhataravartitvād doṣasamudāyād
                        apraśastavyadhād vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra vartim
                        upahṛtyāśu madhukairaṇḍa<pc> </pc>mūla<pc> </pc>mañjiṣṭhā<pc
                            > </pc>yava<pc> </pc>tila<pc> </pc>kalkair madhughṛtapragāḍhair ālepayet
                        tāvad yāvat surūḍha iti surūḍhaṃ cainaṃ punar vidhyet vidhānaṃ tu pūrvoktam
                        eva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.7">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.8">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.9">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra samāsena pañcadaśakarṇabandhākṛtayaḥ | tad yathā nemisandhānaka
                        utpalabhedyako vallūraka āsaṅgimo gaṇḍakarṇa āhāryo nirvedhimo vyāyojimaḥ
                        kapāṭasandhiko 'rdhakapāṭasandhikaḥ saṃkṣipto hīnakarṇo vallīkarṇo
                        yaṣṭikarṇaḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | teṣu pṛthulāyatasamobhayapālir nemisandhānakaḥ
                        vṛttāyatasamobhayapālir utpalabhedyakaḥ hrasvavṛttasamobhayapālir vallūrakaḥ
                        abhyantaradīrghaikapālir āsaṅgimaḥ bāhya<pc> </pc>dīrghaikapālir gaṇḍakarṇaḥ
                        | apālir ubhayato 'py āhāryaḥ pīṭhopamapālir ubhayataḥ kṣīṇaputrikāśrito
                        nirvedhimaḥ | sthūlāṇusamaviṣamapālir vyāyojimaḥ | abhyantaradīrghaikapālir
                        itarālpapāliḥ | kapāṭasandhikaḥ bāhyadīrghaikapālir itarālpapālir
                        ardhakapāṭasandhikaḥ | tatra daśaite karṇabandhavikalpāḥ sādhyāḥ teṣāṃ
                        svanāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ | saṃkṣiptādayaḥ pañcāsādhyāḥ |
                        tatra śuṣkaśaṣkulir utsannapālir itarālpapāliḥ saṃkṣiptaḥ anadhiṣṭhānapāliḥ
                        paryantayoḥ kṣīṇamāṃso hīnakarṇaḥ tanuviṣamālpapālir vallīkarṇaḥ
                        grathitamāṃsastabdhasirāsaṃtatasūkṣmapālir yaṣṭikarṇaḥ
                        nirmāṃsasaṃkṣiptāgrālpaśoṇitapāliḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | baddheṣv api tu
                            śopha<pc> </pc>dāha<pc> </pc>rāga<pc> </pc>pāka<pc
                            > </pc>piḍakā<pc> </pc>srāva<pc> </pc>yuktā na siddhim upayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.13">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.14">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ato nyatamaṃ bandhaṃ cikīrṣur agropaharaṇīyoktopasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraṃ
                        viśeṣataś cātropaharet surāmaṇḍaṃ kṣīram udakaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ kapālacūrṇaṃ ceti
                        | tato 'ṅganāṃ puruṣaṃ vā grathitakeśāntaṃ laghubhuktavantam āptaiḥ
                        suparigṛhītaṃ ca kṛtvā bandham upadhārya chedyabhedyalekhyavyadhanair
                        upapannair upapādya karṇaśoṇitam avekṣya duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ veti tatra vātaduṣṭe
                        dhānyāmloṣṇodakābhyāṃ pittaduṣṭe śītodakapayobhyāṃ śleṣmaduṣṭe
                        surāmaṇḍoṣṇodakābhyāṃ prakṣālya karṇau punar avalikhyānunnatam ahīnam
                        aviṣamaṃ ca karṇasandhiṃ sanniveśya sthitaraktaṃ sandadhyāt | tato
                        madhughṛtenābhyajya picuprotayor anyatareṇāvaguṇṭhya sūtreṇānavagāḍhaman
                        atiśithilaṃ ca baddhvā kapālacūrṇenāvakīryācārikam upadiśed dvivraṇīyoktena
                        ca vidhānenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16x">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāśuddharaktam atipravṛttaraktaṃ kṣīṇaraktaṃ vā saṃdadhyāt | sa hi
                        vātaduṣṭe rakte rūḍho 'pi paripuṭanavān pittaduṣṭe dāhapākarāgavedanāvān
                        śleṣmaduṣṭe stabdhaḥ kaṇḍūmān atipravṛttarakte śyāvaśophavān kṣīṇo 'lpamāṃso
                        na vṛddhim upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āmatailena trirātraṃ pariṣecayet trirātrāc ca picuṃ parivartayet | sa yadā
                        surūḍho nirupadravaḥ savarṇo bhavati tadainaṃ śanaiś śanair abhivardhayet |
                        ato 'nyathā saṃrambhadāhapākarāgavedanāvān punaś chidyate vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāsyāpraduṣṭasyābhivardhanārtham abhyaṅgaḥ | tad yathā
                        godhāpratudaviṣkirānūpaudakavasāmajjānau payaḥ sarpis tailaṃ gaurasarṣapajaṃ
                        ca yathālābhaṃ
                        saṃbhṛtyārkālarkabalātibalānantāpāmārgāśvagandhāvidārigandhākṣīraśuklājalaśūkamadhuravargapayasyāprativāpaṃ
                        tailaṃ vā pācayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sveditonmarditaṃ karṇaṃ snehenaitena yojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ato 'nupadravaḥ samyag balavāṃś ca vivardhate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yavāśvagandhāyaṣṭyāhvais tilaiś codvartanaṃ hitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvaryaśvagandhābhyāṃ payasyair aṇḍajīvanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sakṣīram abhyaṅgāt pālivardhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ye tu karṇā na vardhante svedasnehopapāditāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣām apāṅgadeśe tu kuryāt pracchānam eva tu |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.23b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bāhyacchedaṃ na kurvīta vyāpadaḥ syus tato dhruvāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         baddhamātraṃ tu yaḥ karṇaṃ sahasaivābhivardhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmakośī samādhmātaḥ kṣipram eva vimucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jātaromā suvartmā ca śliṣṭasandhiḥ samaḥ sthiraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         surūḍho 'vedano yaś ca taṃ karṇaṃ vardhayec chanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.0">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.0</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amitāḥ karṇabandhās tu vijñeyāḥ kuśalair iha |
                        <caesura/>
                         yo yathā suviśiṣṭaḥ syāt taṃ tathā viniyojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         (karṇapālyāmayān nṝṇāṃ punar vakṣyāmi suśruta |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇapalyāṃ prakupaitā vātapittakaphās trayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvidhā vāpy atha saṃsṛṣṭāḥ kurvanti vividhā rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         visphoṭaḥ stabdhatā śophaḥ pālyāṃ doṣe tu vātike || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhavisphoṭajananaṃ śophaḥ pākaś ca paittike |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇḍūḥ saśvayathuḥ stambho gurutvaṃ ca kaphātmake || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādoṣaṃ ca saṃśodhya kuryāt teṣāṃ cikitsitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedābhyaṅgaparīṣekaiḥ pralepāsṛgvimokṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdvīṃ kriyāṃ bṛṃhaṇīyair yathāsvaṃ bhojanais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ya evaṃ vetti doṣāṇāṃ cikitsāṃ kartum arhati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ nāmaliṅgair vakṣye pālyām upadravān |
                        <caesura/>
                         atpāṭakaś cotpuṭakaḥ śyāvaḥ kaṇḍūyuto bhṛśam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avamanthaḥ sakaṇḍūko granthiko jambulas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         srāvī ca dāhavāṃś caiva śṛṇveṣāṃ kramaśaḥ kriyām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apāmārgaḥ sarjarasaḥ pāṭalālakucatvacau |
                        <caesura/>
                         utpāṭake pralepaḥ syāt tailam ebhiś ca pācayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śampākaśigrupūtīkān godhāmedo 'tha tadvasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         vārāhaṃ gavyam aiṇeyaṃ pittaṃ sarpiś ca saṃsṛjet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lepam utpuṭake dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaurīṃ sugandhāṃ saśyāmām anantāṃ taṇḍulīyakam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāve pralepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭhāṃ rasāñjanaṃ kṣaudraṃ tathā syād uṣṇakāñjikam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyāl lepaṃ sakaṇḍūke tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇībhūtasya deyaṃ syād idaṃ tailaṃ vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhukakṣīrakākolījīvakādyair vipācitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         godhāvarāhasarpāṇāṃ vasāḥ syuḥ kṛtabṛṃhaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pralepanam idaṃ dadyād avasicyāvamanthake |
                        <caesura/>
                         prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ samaṅgāṃ dhavam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailam ebhiś ca saṃpakvaṃ śṛṇu kaṇḍūmataḥ kriyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahadevā viśvadevā ajākṣīraṃ sasaindhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair ālepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         granthike guṭikāṃ pūrvaṃ srāvayed avapāṭya tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ saindhavacūrṇaṃ tu ghṛṣṭvā lepaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         likhitvā tatsrutaṃ ghṛṣṭvā cūrṇair lodhrasya jambule |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīreṇa pratisāryainaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃropayet tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhuparṇī madhūkaṃ ca ma madhukaṃ madhunā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         lepaḥ srāviṇi dātavyas tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcavalkaiḥ samadhukaiḥ piṣṭais taiś ca ghṛtānvitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvakādyaiḥ sasarpiṣkair dahyamānaṃ pralepayet ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśleṣitāyās tv atha nāsikāyā
                        <caesura/>
                         vakṣyāmi sandhānavidhiṃ yathāvat |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāpramāṇaṃ pṛthivīruhāṇāṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         patraṃ gṛhītvā tv avalambi tasya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tena pramāṇena hi gaṇḍapārśvād
                        <caesura/>
                         utkṛtya baddhaṃ tv atha nāsikāgram |
                        <caesura/>
                         vilikhya cāśu pratisaṃdadhīta
                        <caesura/>
                         tat sādhubandhair bhiṣag apramattaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         susaṃhitaṃ samyag ato yathāvan
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīdvayenābhisamīkṣya baddhvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pronnamya cainām avacūrṇayet tu
                        <caesura/>
                         pataṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāñjanaiś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃchādya samyak picunā sitena
                        <caesura/>
                         tailena siñced asakṛt tilānām |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ ca pāyyaḥ sa naraḥ sujīrṇe
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho virecyaḥ sa yathopadeśam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūḍhaṃ ca sandhānam upāgataṃ syāt
                        <caesura/>
                         tad ardhaśeṣaṃ tu punar nikṛntet |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāṃ punar vardhayituṃ yateta
                        <caesura/>
                         samāṃ ca kuryād ativṛddhamāṃsām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.32">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         ya evam eva jānīyāt sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>

                <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta āmapakvaiṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śophasamutthānā granthividradhyalajīprabhṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyādhayo 'bhihitā
                        anekākṛtayaḥ tair vilakṣaṇaḥ pṛthurgrathitaḥ samo viṣamo vā tvaṅnāṃsasthāyī
                        doṣasaṃghātaḥ śarīraikadeśotthitaḥ śopha ity ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa ṣaḍvidho vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātāgantunimittaḥ | tasya
                        doṣarūpavyañjanair lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra vātaśopho 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
                        paruṣo mṛduranavasthitāstodāyaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti pittaśophaḥ pīto
                        mṛduḥ sarakto vā śīghrānusāryoṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti
                        śleṣmaśophaḥ pāṇḍuḥ śuklo vā kaṭhinaḥ śitaḥ snigdho mandānusārī kaṇḍvādayaś
                        cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti sarvavarṇavedanaḥ sannipātajaḥ pittavacchoṇitajo
                        'tikṛṣṇaś ca pittaraktalakṣaṇa āganturlohitāvabhāsaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa yadā bāhyābhyantaraiḥ kriyāviśeṣair na saṃbhāvitaḥ praśamayituṃ
                        kriyāviparyayādbahutvād vā doṣāṇāṃ tadā pākābhimukho bhavati | tasyāmsya
                        pacyamānasya pakvasya ca lakṣaṇamucyamānam upadhāraya | tatra mandoṣmatā
                        tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthairyaṃ mandavedanatā'lpaśophatā
                        cāmalakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ sūcibhir iva nistudyate daśyata iva pipīlikābhis tābhiś
                        ca saṃsarpyata iva chidyata iva śastreṇa bhidyata iva śaktibhis tāḍyata iva
                        daṇḍena pīḍyata iva pāṇinā ghaṭyata iva cāṅgulyā dahyate pacyata iva
                        cāgnikṣārābhyāṃ oṣacoṣaparīdāhāś ca bhavanti vṛś cikaviddha iva ca
                        sthānāsanaśayaneṣu na śāntim upaiti ādhmātabastirivātataś ca śopho bhavati
                        tvagvaivarṇyaṃ śophābhivṛddhirjvaradāhapipāsā bhaktāruciś ca pacyamānaliṅgaṃ
                        vedanopaśāntiḥ pāṇḍutā'lpaśophatā valīprādurbhāvastvakparipuṭanaṃ
                        nimnadarśanamaṅgulyā'vapīḍite pratyunnamanaṃ bastāvivodakasaṃcaraṇaṃ pūyasya
                        prapīḍayatyekamantamante vā'vapīḍite muhurmuhustodaḥ kaṇḍūrunnatatā vyādher
                        upadravaśāntirbhaktābhikāṅkṣā ca pakvaliṅgam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphajeṣu tu rogeṣu gambhīragatitvād abhighātajeṣu vā keṣucid asamastaṃ
                        pakvalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā pakvam apakvam iti manyamāno bhiṣaṅnoham upaiti | yatra
                        hi tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthaulyamalparujatā'śmavac ca ghanatā na tatra
                        moham upeyād iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmaṃ vipacyamānaṃ ca samyak pakvaṃ ca yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         jānīyāt sa bhaved vaidyaḥ śeṣās taskaravṛttayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātādṛte nāsti rujā na pākaḥ pittādṛte nāsti kaphāc ca pūyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt samastāḥ paripākakāle pacanti śophāṃs traya eva doṣāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kālāntareṇābhyuditaṃ tu pittaṃ kṛtvā vaśe vātakaphau prasahya |
                        <caesura/>
                         pacaty ataḥ śoṇitam eva pāko mato 'pareṣāṃ viduṣāṃ dvitīyaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra āmacchede māṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhivyāpādanam atimātraṃ
                        śoṇitātipravṛttir vedanāprādurbhāvo 'vadaraṇam anekopadravadarśanaṃ
                        kṣatavidradhirvā bhavati | sa yadā bhayamohābhyāṃ pakvam apy apakvam iti
                        manyamānaś ciram upekṣate vyādhiṃ vaidyas tadā gambhīrānugato dvāram
                        alabhamānaḥ pūyaḥ svam āśrayam avadā(ā.dī)ryotasaṅgaṃ mahāntam avakāśaṃ
                        kṛtvā nāḍīṃ janayitvā kṛcchrasādhyo bhavaty asādhyo veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaś chinatty āmam ajñānād yaś ca pakvam upekṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvapacāv iva mantavyau tāv aniścitakāriṇau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāk śastrakarmaṇaś ceṣṭaṃ bhojayed āturaṃ bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         madyapaṃ pāyayen madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yo vedanāsahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na mūrcchaty annasaṃyogān mattaḥ śastraṃ na budhyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād avaśyaṃ bhoktavyaṃ rogeṣūkteṣu karmaṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāṇo hy ābhyantaro nṇṇāṃ bāhyaprāṇaguṇānvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhārayaty avirodhena śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alpo mahān vā kriyayā vinā yaḥ samucchritaḥ pākam upaiti śophaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśālamūlo viṣamo vidagdhaḥ sa kṛcchritāṃ yāty avagāḍhadoṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ālepavisrāvaṇaśodhanais tu samyak prayukair yadi nopaśāmyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pacyet śīghraṃ samam alpamūlaḥ sa piṇḍitaś copari connataḥ syāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kakṣaṃ samāsādya yathaiva vahnir vāte(ā.yvī)ritaḥ saṃdahati prasahya |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathaiva pūyo 'py aviniḥsṛto hi māṃsaṃ sirāḥ snāyu ca khādatīha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādau vimlāpanaṃ kuryād dvitīyam avasecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛtīyam upanāhaṃ tu caturthīṃ pāṭanakriyām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcamaṃ śodhanaṃ kuryāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete kramā vraṇasyoktāḥ saptamaṃ vaikṛtāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.trailer">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āmapakvaiṣaṇīyo 'nāma saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        || </l>
                </div>


                <div n="18" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.2">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ālipa ādya upakramaḥ eṣa sarvaśophānāṃ sāmānyaḥ pradhānatamaś ca taṃ ca
                        pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tato bandhaḥ pradhānaṃ tena
                        śuddhirvraṇaropaṇamasthisaṃdhisthairyaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pratilomamālimpennānulomam | pratilome hi samyagauṣadhamavatiṣṭhate
                        'nupraviśati romakūpān svedavāhibhiś ca sirāmukhairvīryaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca śuṣyamāṇamupekṣeta anyatra pīḍayitavyāt śuṣko hy apārthako rukkaraś
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa trividhaḥ pralepaḥ pradeha ālepaś ca | teṣām antaraṃ pralepaḥ śītas
                        tanur aviśoṣī viśoṣī ca pradehas tūṣṇaḥ śīto vā bahalo 'bahur aviśoṣī ca
                        madhaymo 'trālepaḥ | tatra raktapittaprasādakṛd ālepaḥ pradeho
                        vātaśleṣmapraśamanaḥ saṃdhānaḥ śodhano ropaṇaḥ śophavedanāpahaś ca
                        tasyopayogaḥ kṣatākṣateṣu yas tu kṣateṣūpayujyate sa bhūyaḥ kalka iti
                        saṃjñāṃ labhate niruddālepanasaṃjñaḥ tenāsrāvasannirodho mṛdutā
                        pūtimāṃsāpakarṣaṇam anantardoṣatā vraṇaśuddhiś ca bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avidagdheṣu śopheṣu hitam ālepanaṃ bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāsvaṃ doṣaśamanaṃ dāhakaṇḍūrujāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tvakprasādanam evāgryaṃ māṃsaraktaprasādanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhapraśamanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ todakaṇḍūvināśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         marmadeśeṣu ye togā guhyeṣv api tathā nṛām |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhanāya teṣāṃ hi kuryād ālepanaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         (?ṣaḍbhāgaṃ paittike snehaṃ catrubhāgaṃ tu vātike |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭabhāgaṃ tu kaphaje snehamātrāṃ pradāpayet ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya pramāṇamārdramāhiṣacarmotsedham upadiśanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na cālepaṃ rātrau prayuñjīta mābhūc chaityapihitoṣmaṇas tad anirgamād
                        vikārapravṛtti(ā.ddhi)r iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pradehasādhye vyādhau tu hitam ālepanaṃ divā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaraktābhighātotthe saviṣe ca viśeṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca paryuṣitaṃ lepaṃ kadācidavacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         upary upari lepaṃ tu na kadācit pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ūṣmāṇaṃ vedanāṃ dāhaṃ ghanatvājjanayet sa hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca tenaiva lepena pradehaṃ dāpayet punaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.15ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣkabhāvāt sa nirvīryo yukto 'pi syād apārthakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ vraṇabandhanadravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ tad yathā
                        kṣaumakārpāsāvikadukūlakauśeyapatrorṇacīnapaṭṭacarmāntarvalkalālābūśakalalatāvidalarajjutūlaphalasantānikālauhānīti
                        teṣaṃ vyādhiṃ kālaṃ cāvekṣyopayogaḥ prakaraṇataś caiṣām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        kośadāmasvastikānuvellitapra(ā.mu)tolīmaṇḍalasthagikāyamakakhaṭvācīnavibandhavitānagophaṇāḥ
                        pañcāṅgī ceti caturdaśa bandhaviśeṣāḥ | teṣāṃ nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa
                        vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kośamaṅguṣṭhāṅguliparvasu vidadhyāt dāmasaṃbādhe 'ṅge
                        sandhikūrcakabhrūstanāntaratalakarṇeṣu svastikaṃ anuvellitaṃ tu śākhāsu
                        grīvāmeḍhrayoḥ pratolīṃ vṛtte 'ṅge maṇḍalaṃ aṅguṣṭhāṅgulimeḍhrāgreṣu
                        sthagikāṃ yamalavraṇayor yamakaṃ hanuśaṅkhagaṇḍeṣu khaṭvāṃ apāṅgayoś cīnaṃ
                        pṛṣṭhodaroraḥsu vibandhaṃ mūrdhani vitānaṃ cibukanāsauṣṭhāṃsabastiṣu
                        gophaṇāṃ jatruṇa ūrdhvaṃ pañcāṅgīm iti yo vā yasmin śarīrapradeśe suniviṣṭo
                        bhavati taṃ tasmin vidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yantraṇam ūrdhvamadhistiryak ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā vāmahastaparikṣepamṛjum anāviddham
                        asaṃkucitaṃ mṛdu paṭṭaṃ niveśya badhnīyāt | na ca vraṇasyopari kuryād
                        granthim ābādhakaraṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.21</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        kledo raukṣyāc chedo durnyāsāhraṇavartmāvagharṣaṇam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vraṇayatanaviśeṣād bandhaviśeṣas trividho bhavati gāḍhaḥ samaḥ
                        śithila iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pīḍayann arujo gāḍhaḥ socchvāsaḥ śithilaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naiva gāḍho na śithilaḥ samo bandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sphikkukṣikakṣāvaṅkṣaṇoruśiraḥsu gāḍhaḥ
                        śākhāvadanakarṇakaṇṭhameḍhramuṣkapṛṣṭhapārśvodaroraḥsu samaḥ akṣṇoḥ sandhiṣu
                        ca śithila ti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra paittikaṃ gāḍhasthāne samaṃ badhnīyāt samasthāne śithilaṃ
                        śithilasthāne naiva evaṃ śoṇitaduṣṭaṃ ca ślaiṣmikaṃ śithilasthāne samaṃ
                        samasthāne gāḍhaṃ gāḍhasthāne gāḍhataraṃ evaṃ vātaduṣṭaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra paittikaṃ śaradi grīṣme dvirahno badhnīyāt raktopadrutamapyevaṃ
                        ślaiṣmikaṃ hemantavasantayostryahāt vātopadrutamapyevam | evamabhyūhya
                        bandhaviparyayaṃ ca kuryāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra samaśithilasthāneṣu gāḍhaṃ baddhe vikeśikauṣadhanair arthakyaṃ
                        śophavedanāprādurbhāvaś ca gāḍhasamasthāneṣu śithilaṃ baddhe
                        vikeśikauṣadhapatanaṃ paṭṭasaṃcārāhraṇavartmāvagharṣanam iti
                        gāḍhaśithilasthāneṣu samaṃ baddhe ca guṇābhāva iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.28</label>
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abadhyamāno daṃśamaśakatṛṇakāṣṭhopalapāṃśuśītavātātapaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair
                        abhihanyate vraṇo vividhavedanopadrutaś ca duṣṭatām upaity ālepanādīni cāsya
                        viśoṣam upayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.30">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.31">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.32">

                        <caesura/>

                        prakuthitapraśīrṇamāṃsāś ca bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.33">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.34">

                        <caesura/>
                         māṃsāpāke na badhyante gudapāke ca dāruṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         svabuddhyā cāpi vibhajet kṛtyākṛtyāṃś ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         deśaṃ doṣaṃ ca vijñāya vraṇaṃ ca vraṇakovidaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛtūṃś ca parisaṃkhyāya tato bandhān niveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrdhvaṃ tiryag adhastāc ca yantraṇā trividhā smṛtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ca badhyate bandhas tathā vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā mṛdu caivāpi paṭṭakam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakledayatyatisnigdhā tathā rūkṣā kṣiṇoti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktasnehā ropayati durnyastā vartma gharṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣamaṃ ca vraṇaṃ kuryāt stambhayet srāvayet tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāvraṇaṃ viditvā tu yogaṃ vaidyaḥ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaje raktaje vā'pi sakṛteva parikṣipet |
                        <caesura/>
                         asakṛt kaphaje vā'pi vātaje ca vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         talena pratipīḍyātha srāvayed anulomataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvāṃś ca bandhān gūḍhāntān sandhīṃś ca viniveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.42">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.42</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         buddhyotprekṣyābhiyuktena tathā cāsthiṣu jānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.43">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uttiṣṭhato niṣaṇṇasya śayanaṃ vā'dhigacchataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gacchato vividhair yānair nāsya duṣyati sa vraṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.44">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye ca syur māṃsasaṃsthā vai tvaggatāś ca tathā vraṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhyasthikoṣṭhaprāptāś ca sirāsnāyugatās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.45">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā'vagāḍhagambhīrāḥ sarvato viṣamasthitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.2">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇitasya prathamamevāgāramanvicchet taccāgāraṃ praśastavāstvād ikaṃ
                        karyam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastavāstuni gṛhe śucāvātapavarjite |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivāte na ca rogāḥ syuḥ śārīrāgantumānasāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin śayanamasaṃbādhaṃ svāstīrṇaṃ manojñaṃ prākśiraskaṃ saśastraṃ kurvīt
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaceṣṭāpracāraḥ syāt svāstīrṇe śayane vraṇī |
                        <caesura/>
                         prācyāṃ diśi sthitā devāstatpūjārthaṃ ca tacchiraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin suhṛdbhir anukūlaiḥ priyaṃvadair upāsyamāno yatheṣṭamāsīt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         suhṛdo vikṣipantyāśu kathābhir vraṇavedanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āśvāsayanto bahuśastvanukūlāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca divānidrāvaśagaḥ syāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         divāsvapnāddraṇe kaṇḍūrgātrāṇāṃ gauravaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvayathurvedanā rāgaḥ srāvaś caiva bhṛśaṃ bhavet ||// </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         utthānasaṃveśanaparivartanacaṅkramaṇoccair bhāṣaṇādyāsvātmaceṣṭāsvapramatto
                        vraṇaṃ saṃrakṣet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānāsanaṃ caṅkramaṇaṃ divāsvapnaṃ tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇito na niṣeveta śaktimān api mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         utthānādyāsanaṃ sthānaṃ śayyā cātiniṣevitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāpnuyānmārutādaṅge rujastasmād vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gamyānāṃ ca strīṇāṃ saṃdarśanasaṃbhāṣaṇasaṃsparśanāni dūrataḥ pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         strīdarśanādibhiḥ śukraṃ kadāciccalitaṃ sravet |
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyadharmakṛtāndoṣān so 'saṃsarge 'pyavāpnuyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         navadhānyamāṣatilakalāyakulatthaniṣpāvaharitakaśākāmlalavaṇakaṭukaguḍapiṣṭavikṛtivallūraśuṣkaśākājāvikānūpaudakamāṃsavasāśītodakakṛśarāpāyasadadhidugdhatakraprabhṛtīn
                        pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.17">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         doṣasaṃjanano hyeṣa vijñeyaḥ pūyavardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.18">

                        <caesura/>
                         madyapaś ca maireyāriṣṭāsavaśīdhusurāvikārān pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.19">

                        <caesura/>
                         āśukāri ca tat pītaṃ kṣipraṃ vyāpādayed draṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātātaparajodhūmāvaśyāyātisevanātibhojanāniṣṭabhojanāśravaṇadarśanerṣyāmarṣabhayakrodhaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇaviṣamāśanaśayanopavāsavāgvyāyāmasthānacaṅkramaṇaśītavātaviruddhādhyaśanājīrṇamakṣikādyā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.21">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.22">

                        <caesura/>
