                         yasya chardir vireko vā daśanāḥ prapatanti vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śālmalīṃ kiṃśukaṃ yūpaṃ valmīkaṃ pāribhadrakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.65">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.65</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         puṣpāḍhyaṃ kovidāraṃ vā citāṃ vā yo 'dhirohati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kārpāsatailapiṇyākalohāni lavaṇaṃ tilān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.66">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.66</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         labhetāśnīta vā pakvam annaṃ yaś ca pibet surām |
                        <caesura/>
                         svasthaḥ sa labhate vyādhiṃ vyādhito mṛtyum ṛcchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.67">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.67</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāsvaṃ prakṛtisvapno vismṛto vihatas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cintākṛto divā dṛṣto bhavanty aphaladās tu te || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.68">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.68</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jvaritānāṃ śunā sakhyaṃ kapisakhyaṃ tu śoṣiṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         unmāde rākṣasaiḥ pretair apasmāre pravartanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.69">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.69</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mehātisāriṇāṃ toyapānaṃ snehasya kuṣṭhinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         gulmeṣu sthāvarotpattiḥ koṣṭhe mūrdhni śiroruji || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.70">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.70</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṣkulībhakṣaṇaṃ chardyāmadhvā śvāsapipāsayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haridraṃ bhojanaṃ vā'pi yasya syāt pāṇḍurogiṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.71">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.71</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         raktapittī pibed yas tu śoṇitaṃ sa vinaśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         svapnānevaṃvidhān dṛṣṭvā prātarutthāya yatnavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.72">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.72</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyānmāṣāṃstilāṃllohaṃ viprebhyaḥ kāñcanaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         japec cāpi śubhān mantrān gāyatrīṃ tripadāṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.73">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.73</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭvā tu prathame yāme svapyād dhyātvā punaḥ śubham |
                        <caesura/>
                         japedvā'nyatamaṃ vede brahmacārī samāhitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.74">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.74</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         devatāyatane caiva vasedrātritrayaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viprāṃś ca pūjayennityaṃ duḥsvapnāt pravimucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.75">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.75</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśastaṃ svapnadarśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         devān dvijān govṛṣabhān jīvataḥ suhṛdo nṛpān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.76">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.76</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samiddham agniṃ sādhūṃś ca nirmalāni jalāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         paśyet kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.77">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.77</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māṃsaṃ matsyān srajaḥ śvetā vāsāṃsi ca phalāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         labhante dhanalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.78">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.78</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mahāprāsādasaphalavṛkṣavāraṇaparvatān |
                        <caesura/>
                         āroheddravyalābhāya vyādherapagamāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.79</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca kṣubhitān kaluṣodakān |
                        <caesura/>
                         taret kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.80">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.80</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         urago vā jalauko vā bhramaro vā'pi yaṃ daśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ārogyaṃ nirdiśettasya dhanalābhaṃ ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.81">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.81</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃrūpān śubhān svapnān yaḥ paśyed vyādhito naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa dīrghāyur iti jñeyas tasmai karma samācaret || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        viparītāviparītasvapnanidarśanīyo nāmaikonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>




                <div n="30" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ pañcendriyārthavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīraśīlayor yasya prakṛter vikṛtir bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tva riṣṭaṃ samāsena vyāsatas tu nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṇoti vividhān śabdān yo divyānām abhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samudrapurameghānām asaṃpattau ca niḥsvanān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tān svanānnāvagṛhṇāti manyate cānyaśabdavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyāraṇyasvanāṃś cāpi viparītān śṛṇoti ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣacchabdeṣu ramate suhṛcchabdeṣu kupyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         na śṛṇoti ca yo 'kasmāttaṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tūṣṇam iva gṛhṇāti śītamuṣṇaṃ ca śītavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃjātaśītapiḍako yaś ca dāhena pīḍyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇagātro 'timātraṃ ca yaḥ śītena pravepate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prahārān nābhijānāti yo 'ṅgacchedamathāpi vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṃśunevāvakīrṇāni yaś ca gātrāṇi manyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         varṇānyatā vā rājyo vā yasya gātre bhavanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snātānuliptaṃ yaṃ cāpi bhajante nīlamakṣikāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sugandhirvā'ti yo 'kasmāt taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viparītena gṛhṇāti rasān yaś copayojitān |
                        <caesura/>
                         upayuktāḥ kramādyasya rasā doṣābhivṛddhaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya doṣāgnisāmyaṃ ca kuryur mithyopayojitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vā rasān na saṃvetti gatāsuṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sugandhaṃ vetti durgandhaṃ durgandhasya sugandhitām |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhṇīte vā 'nyathā gandhaṃ śānte dīpe ca nīrujaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vā gandhān na jānāti gatāsuṃ taṃ vinirdiśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvandvānyuṣṇahimādīni kālāvasthā diśas tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viparītena gṛhṇāti bhāvān anyāṃś ca yo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         divā jyotīṃṣi yaś cāpi jvalitānīva paśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rātrau sūryaṃ jvalantaṃ vā divā vā candravarcasam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ameghopaplave yaś ca śakracāpataḍidguṇān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taḍittvato 'sitān yo vā nirmale gagane ghanān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vimānayānaprāsādair yaś ca saṃkulamambaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yaś cānilaṃ mūrtimantam antarikṣaṃ ca paśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmanīhāravāsobhir āvṛtām iva medinīm || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pradīptam iva lokaṃ ca yo vā plutam ivāmbhasā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūmim aṣṭāpadākārāṃ lekhābhir yaś ca paśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na paśyati sanakṣatrāṃ yaś cā devīm arundhatīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhruvam ākāśagaṅgāṃ vā taṃ vadanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jyotsnādarśoṣṇatoyeṣu chāyāṃ yaś ca na paśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         paśyaty ekāṅgahīnāṃ vā vikṛtāṃ vā'nyasattvajām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvakākakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ pretānāṃ yakṣarakṣasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         piśācoraganāgānāṃ bhūtānāṃ vikṛtām api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vā mayūrakaṇṭhābhaṃ vidhūmaṃ vahnim īkṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         āturasya bhaven mṛtyuḥ svastho vyādhim āvāpnuyāt || </l>


                    <p xml:id="SS.1.30.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        pañcendriyārthavipratipattir nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>


                <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaś chāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāvā lohitikā nīlā pītikā vā'pi mānavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhidravanti yaṃ chāyāḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hrīr apakramate yasya prabhādhṛtismṛtiśriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         akasmād yaṃ bhajante vā sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhvaṃ tathottaraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āraktā daśanā yasya śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         khañjanapratimā vā'pi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇā stabdhā'valiptā vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         karkaśā vā bhavedyasya so 'cirād vijahāty asūn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṭilā sphuṭitā vā'pi śuṣkā vā yasya nāsikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         avasphūrjati magnā vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃkṣipte viṣame stabdhe rakte sraste ca locane |
                        <caesura/>
                         syātāṃ vā prasrute yasya sa gatāyurnaro dhruvam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         keśāḥ sīmantino yasya saṃkṣipte vinate bhruvau |
                        <caesura/>
                         lunanti cākṣipakṣmāṇi so 'cirādyāti mṛtyave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāharaty annam āsyasthaṃ na dhārayati yaḥ śiraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balavān durbalo vā'pi saṃmohaṃ yo 'dhigacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         utthāpyamāno bahuśastaṃ pakvaṃ bhiṣagādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uttānaḥ sarvadā śete pādau vikurute ca yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viprasāraṇaśīlo vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītapādakarocchvāsaś chinnocchvāsaś ca yo bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyas taṃ dhīraḥ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nidrā na chidyate yasya yo vā jāgarti sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         muhyed vā vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uttarauṣṭhaṃ ca yo lihyād utkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ pretarūpaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svebhyaḥ saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣasyāviṣārtasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātāṣṭhīlā tu hṛdaye yasyor dhvam anuyāyinī |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujā'nnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ananyopadravakṛtaḥ śophaḥ pādasamutthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣaṃ hanti nārīṃ tu mukhajo guhyajo dvayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atisāro jvaro hikkā chardiḥ śūnāṇḍameḍhratā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsinaḥ kāsino vā'pi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedo dāhaś ca balavān hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         balavantam api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāvā jihvā bhaved yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhaṃ ca jāyate pūti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaktram āpūryate 'śrubhiḥ svidyataś caraṇāv ubhau |
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atimātraṃ laghūni syur gātrāṇi gurukāṇi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā vaivasvatālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gantāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yūkā lalāṭam āyānti baliṃ nāśnanti vāyasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yeṣāṃ vā'pi ratir nāsti yātāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jvarātisāraśophāḥ syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya nāsau śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇasya yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair miṣṭair hitais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         na śāmyato 'nnapānaiś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṃ koṣṭhaśūlaṃ ca dāruṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pipāsā balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anityatvāc ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanaṃ vrajet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pretā bhūtāḥ piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         maraṇābhimukhaṃ nityam upasarpanti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi pratighnanti jighāṃsayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmān moghāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā bhavanty eva gatāyuṣām || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        chāyāvipratipattirnāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                </div>



            </div>
        </body>
    </text>
</TEI>
